[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview#introduction)

Introduction
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to **Bridge**, the seamless way to integrate stablecoin payments into your product. Bridge lets you move money with internet speed and global reach — across fiat rails and stablecoins. Whether you’re building global payment flows, launching a card product, or managing wallets, Bridge offers a composable set of APIs to power seamless money movement. This guide is designed to help you navigate our APIs, avoid common integration pitfalls, and get to market faster.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview#what-you-can-build-with-bridge)

What you can build with Bridge
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Send & receive payments**  
    Move funds globally using fiat rails, stablecoins, or supported digital assets.
*   **Virtual accounts**  
    Instantly issue USD, EUR, and MXN deposit accounts for your users with local bank details.
*   **Custody funds**  
    Provision custodial wallets to hold stablecoin balances securely.
*   **Issue stablecoins**  
    Launch your own branded stablecoin or use USDB to earn rewards on held balances.
*   **Issue cards**  
    Enable users to spend from their stablecoin balances with Visa-powered virtual cards.

* * *

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview#get-started)

Get started
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s a quick guide to help you find what you need:

[Get started\
-----------\
\
Get up and running with our API in minutes.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/get-set-up-with-bridge)

[Guides\
------\
\
Explore starter core use cases for moving money using orchestration, wallets, cards, and more.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides)

[Developer Platform\
------------------\
\
More detailed documentation on the developer platform.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform)

[API Reference\
-------------\
\
Detailed endpoint documentation with request/response schemas.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference)

[Changelog\
---------\
\
Read more about recent feature improvements and launches.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview#key-platform-components)

Key platform components
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Bridge developer platform includes flexible and simple APIs to power your use cases.

[Customers\
---------\
\
Easily onboard users with KYC/KYB flows and manage identity lifecycle.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/customers)

[Orchestration\
-------------\
\
APIs to send, receive, and convert between fiat and stablecoins. Power on ramps, off ramps, and crypto to crypto payments using transfers.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration)

[Wallets\
-------\
\
Custody funds for your customers or your company, initiate transfers, and check balances with secure custodial wallets.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/wallets)

[Issuance\
--------\
\
Launch your own branded stablecoin and earn on-chain rewards on balances held in Bridge-issued stablecoins.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/issuance)

[Cards\
-----\
\
Issue branded Visa cards that work online, in-store, and through mobile wallets. Customers can spend directly from stablecoin balances.](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/cards)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview#getting-help)

Getting Help
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’re excited to have you build with us! If you have questions, run into issues, or just want to say hi, you can contact us at [support@bridge.xyz](mailto:support@bridge.xyz)
 or visit our [Support Page](https://support.bridge.xyz/)

Associated Persons

Get a single associated person

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Get a single associated person

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/associated_persons/{associatedPersonID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulAssociatedPersonResponse

    {
      "id": "associated_person_1234567890",
      "email": "associated_person@business.co",
      "first_name": "John",
      "last_name": "Smith",
      "has_ownership": true,
      "has_control": true,
      "is_signer": true,
      "title": "Chief Executive Officer",
      "relationship_established_at": "2025-05-27T17:55:33.308Z",
      "created_at": "2025-05-27T17:55:33.308Z",
      "updated_at": "2025-05-27T17:55:33.308Z"
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#parameter-associated-person-id)

associatedPersonID

string

required

Unique identifier for an associated person A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Response

200

application/json

Successful associated person response

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-id)

id

string

required

Unique identifier for the associated person

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-created-at)

created\_at

integer

required

Created timestamp in milliseconds since Unix epoch

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

integer

required

Last updated timestamp in milliseconds since Unix epoch

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-email)

email

string

The email address of the associated person

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-first-name)

first\_name

string

The first name of the associated person

Required string length: `2 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-last-name)

last\_name

string

The last name of the associated person

Required string length: `2 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-has-ownership)

has\_ownership

boolean

True if this person has at least 25% ownership of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-has-control)

has\_control

boolean

True if this is the control person of the company, having significant responsibility to control, manage or influence the activities of the business entity.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-is-signer)

is\_signer

boolean

True if this person is able to authorize transactions on behalf of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-title)

title

string

The title of this associated person at the company, e.g. CEO, CFO, etc.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-attested-ownership-structure-at)

attested\_ownership\_structure\_at

string

When this individual attested to the correctness of the ownership structure provided to Bridge. If provided by at least one control person, ownership documents for the business are not required.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/get-a-single-associated-person#response-relationship-established-at)

relationship\_established\_at

string

When the associated person relationship was established in format yyyy-mm-dd.

cURL

      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

# Create a Batch Settlement Schedule - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/batch-settlements/create-a-batch-settlement-schedule#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Batch Settlements

Create a Batch Settlement Schedule

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Create a Batch Settlement Schedule

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/batch_settlement_schedules \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "destination": {
        "currency": "brl",
        "payment_rail": "ach",
        "external_account_id": "<string>",
        "bridge_wallet_id": "<string>",
        "wire_message": "<string>",
        "sepa_reference": "<string>",
        "swift_reference": "<string>",
        "spei_reference": "<string>",
        "reference": "<string>",
        "swift_charges": "our",
        "ach_reference": "<string>",
        "blockchain_memo": "<string>",
        "deposit_id": "<string>"
      }
    }
    '

200

Example

    {
      "id": "<string>"
    }

POST

/

customers

/

{customerID}

/

batch\_settlement\_schedules

Try it

Create a Batch Settlement Schedule

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/batch_settlement_schedules \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "destination": {
        "currency": "brl",
        "payment_rail": "ach",
        "external_account_id": "<string>",
        "bridge_wallet_id": "<string>",
        "wire_message": "<string>",
        "sepa_reference": "<string>",
        "swift_reference": "<string>",
        "spei_reference": "<string>",
        "reference": "<string>",
        "swift_charges": "our",
        "ach_reference": "<string>",
        "blockchain_memo": "<string>",
        "deposit_id": "<string>"
      }
    }
    '

200

Example

    {
      "id": "<string>"
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/batch-settlements/create-a-batch-settlement-schedule#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Headers

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/batch-settlements/create-a-batch-settlement-schedule#parameter-idempotency-key)

Idempotency-Key

string

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/batch-settlements/create-a-batch-settlement-schedule#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Body

application/json

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/batch-settlements/create-a-batch-settlement-schedule#body-destination)

destination

object

required

The destination that Bridge will use to settle funds.

Show child attributes

#### Response

200

application/json

Batch Settlement Schedule object created

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/batch-settlements/create-a-batch-settlement-schedule#response-id)

id

string

required

ID of the batch settlement schedule

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

Associated Persons

Update a single associated person

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Update a single associated person

cURL

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/associated_persons/{associatedPersonID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "first_name": "<string>",
      "last_name": "<string>",
      "email": "<string>",
      "residential_address": {
        "street_line_1": "<string>",
        "city": "<string>",
        "country": "<string>",
        "street_line_2": "<string>",
        "subdivision": "<string>",
        "postal_code": "<string>"
      },
      "birth_date": "<string>",
      "has_ownership": true,
      "has_control": true,
      "is_signer": true,
      "identifying_information": [\
        {\
          "type": "drivers_license",\
          "issuing_country": "<string>",\
          "number": "<string>",\
          "description": "<string>",\
          "expiration": "<string>",\
          "image_front": "<string>",\
          "image_back": "<string>"\
        }\
      ],
      "middle_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_first_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_middle_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_last_name": "<string>",
      "phone": "<string>",
      "is_director": true,
      "title": "<string>",
      "ownership_percentage": 123,
      "attested_ownership_structure_at": "<string>",
      "relationship_established_at": "<string>",
      "verified_govid_at": "<string>",
      "verified_selfie_at": "<string>",
      "completed_customer_safety_check_at": "<string>",
      "documents": [\
        {\
          "purposes": [\
            "proof_of_account_purpose"\
          ],\
          "file": "<string>",\
          "description": "<string>"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    '

200

SuccessfulAssociatedPersonResponse

    {
      "id": "associated_person_1234567890",
      "email": "associated_person@business.co",
      "first_name": "John",
      "last_name": "Smith",
      "has_ownership": true,
      "has_control": true,
      "is_signer": true,
      "title": "Chief Executive Officer",
      "relationship_established_at": "2025-05-27T17:55:33.308Z",
      "created_at": "2025-05-27T17:55:33.308Z",
      "updated_at": "2025-05-27T17:55:33.308Z"
    }

      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/associated_persons/{associatedPersonID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \

      "email": "associated_person@business.co",

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#parameter-associated-person-id)

associatedPersonID

string

required

Unique identifier for an associated person A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Body

application/json

Associated person data to update

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-first-name)

first\_name

string

required

The first name of the associated person

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-last-name)

last\_name

string

required

The last name of the associated person

Required string length: `2 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-email)

email

string

required

The persons primary email address

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-residential-address)

residential\_address

object

required

The residential address of the associated person. This must be a physical address and cannot be a PO Box.

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-birth-date)

birth\_date

string

required

Date of birth in format yyyy-mm-dd. Must be at least 18 years old.

Required string length: `10`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-has-ownership)

has\_ownership

boolean

required

True if this person has at least 25% ownership of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-has-control)

has\_control

boolean

required

True if this is the control person of the company, having significant responsibility to control, manage or influence the activities of the business entity. At least one control person must be specified.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-is-signer)

is\_signer

boolean

required

True if this person is able to authorize transactions on behalf of the business. At least one signer must be specified.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-identifying-information)

identifying\_information

Identification Information · object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-middle-name)

middle\_name

string

The middle name of the associated person

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-transliterated-first-name)

transliterated\_first\_name

string

Required when the `first_name` includes any non Latin-1 characters. Acceptable characters - Latin-1 Unicode Character Range: À-ÖØ-ßà-öø-ÿ; Standard Unicode Character Range: -~

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-transliterated-middle-name)

transliterated\_middle\_name

string

Required when the `middle_name` includes any non Latin-1 characters. Acceptable characters - Latin-1 Unicode Character Range: À-ÖØ-ßà-öø-ÿ; Standard Unicode Character Range: -~

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-transliterated-last-name)

transliterated\_last\_name

string

Required when the `last_name` includes any non Latin-1 characters. Acceptable characters - Latin-1 Unicode Character Range: À-ÖØ-ßà-öø-ÿ; Standard Unicode Character Range: -~

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-phone)

phone

string

The persons phone in format "+12223334444"

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-transliterated-residential-address)

transliterated\_residential\_address

object

Required when any part of the `residential_address` includes any non Latin-1 characters. Acceptable characters - Latin-1 Unicode Character Range: À-ÖØ-ßà-öø-ÿ; Standard Unicode Character Range: -~

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-is-director)

is\_director

boolean

True if this person is an appointed director of the company.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-title)

title

string

The title of this associated person at the company, e.g. CEO, CFO, etc. Required if has\_control is true.

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-ownership-percentage)

ownership\_percentage

integer

Ultimate ownership percentage of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-attested-ownership-structure-at)

attested\_ownership\_structure\_at

string

The date or timestamp when this individual attested to the correctness of the ownership structure provided to Bridge. If provided by at least one control person, ownership documents for the business are not required.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-relationship-established-at)

relationship\_established\_at

string

The date or timestamp when the associated person relationship was established in format yyyy-mm-dd.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-verified-govid-at)

verified\_govid\_at

string

The date or timestamp for when individual's government ID was successfully verified.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-verified-selfie-at)

verified\_selfie\_at

string

The date or timestamp for when individual's selfie was successfully verified.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-completed-customer-safety-check-at)

completed\_customer\_safety\_check\_at

string

The date or timestamp for when individual successfully passed customer safety check.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#body-documents)

documents

Documents · object\[\]

Please click "ADD OBJECT" for more information.

Show child attributes

#### Response

200

application/json

Updated associated person

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-id)

id

string

required

Unique identifier for the associated person

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-created-at)

created\_at

integer

required

Created timestamp in milliseconds since Unix epoch

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

integer

required

Last updated timestamp in milliseconds since Unix epoch

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-email)

email

string

The email address of the associated person

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-first-name)

first\_name

string

The first name of the associated person

Required string length: `2 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-last-name)

last\_name

string

The last name of the associated person

Required string length: `2 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-has-ownership)

has\_ownership

boolean

True if this person has at least 25% ownership of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-has-control)

has\_control

boolean

True if this is the control person of the company, having significant responsibility to control, manage or influence the activities of the business entity.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-is-signer)

is\_signer

boolean

True if this person is able to authorize transactions on behalf of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-title)

title

string

The title of this associated person at the company, e.g. CEO, CFO, etc.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-attested-ownership-structure-at)

attested\_ownership\_structure\_at

string

When this individual attested to the correctness of the ownership structure provided to Bridge. If provided by at least one control person, ownership documents for the business are not required.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/associated-persons/update-a-single-associated-person#response-relationship-established-at)

relationship\_established\_at

string

When the associated person relationship was established in format yyyy-mm-dd.

# Create a Bridge Wallet - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Navigation

Bridge Wallets

Create a Bridge Wallet

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Create a Bridge Wallet

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/wallets \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "chain": "base"
    }
    '

201

SuccessfulLiquidationAddressCreateResponse

    {
      "id": "bw_123",
      "chain": "solana",
      "address": "9kV3ZMehKVyxfHKCcaDLye3P9HHw2MP4jtQa2gKBUmCs",
      "created_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",
      "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"
    }

POST

/

customers

/

{customerID}

/

wallets

Create a Bridge Wallet

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/wallets \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "chain": "base"
    }
    '

201

SuccessfulLiquidationAddressCreateResponse

    {
      "id": "bw_123",
      "chain": "solana",
      "address": "9kV3ZMehKVyxfHKCcaDLye3P9HHw2MP4jtQa2gKBUmCs",
      "created_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",
      "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Headers

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#parameter-idempotency-key)

Idempotency-Key

string

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Body

application/json

Bridge Wallet to be created

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#body-chain)

chain

enum<string>

required

Available options:

`base`,

`ethereum`,

`solana`,

`tempo`,

`tron`

#### Response

201

application/json

Bridge Wallet created

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#response-chain)

chain

enum<string>

required

Available options:

`base`,

`ethereum`,

`solana`,

`tempo`,

`tron`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#response-id)

id

string

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#response-address)

address

string

The blockchain address of the Bridge Wallet

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#response-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

Time of creation of the Bridge Wallet

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/create-a-bridge-wallet#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

Time of most recent update of the Bridge Wallet

Get a Bridge Wallet

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/wallets/{bridgeWalletID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulBridgeWalletGetResponse

    {
      "id": "bw_123",
      "chain": "solana",

      "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",

          "balance": "100.25",\

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-a-bridge-wallet#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-a-bridge-wallet#parameter-bridge-wallet-id)

bridgeWalletID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Response

200

application/json

A Bridge Wallet object response

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-a-bridge-wallet#response-chain)

chain

enum<string>

required

The chain of the Bridge Wallet

Available options:

`base`,

`ethereum`,

`solana`,

`tempo`,

`tron`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-a-bridge-wallet#response-id)

id

string

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-a-bridge-wallet#response-address)

address

string

The blockchain address of the Bridge Wallet

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-a-bridge-wallet#response-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

Time of creation of the Bridge Wallet

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-a-bridge-wallet#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

Time of most recent update of the Bridge Wallet

balances

object\[\]

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Bridge Wallets

Get all Bridge Wallets for a customer

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Get all Bridge Wallets for a customer

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/wallets \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulBridgeWalletListResponse

    {
      "count": 1,
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": "bw_123",\
          "chain": "solana",\
          "address": "9kV3ZMehKVyxfHKCcaDLye3P9HHw2MP4jtQa2gKBUmCs",\
          "created_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",\
          "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"\
        }\
      ]
    }

GET

/

customers

/

{customerID}

/

wallets

Try it

Get all Bridge Wallets for a customer

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/wallets \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulBridgeWalletListResponse

    {
      "count": 1,
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": "bw_123",\
          "chain": "solana",\
          "address": "9kV3ZMehKVyxfHKCcaDLye3P9HHw2MP4jtQa2gKBUmCs",\
          "created_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",\
          "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-all-bridge-wallets-for-a-customer#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-all-bridge-wallets-for-a-customer#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-all-bridge-wallets-for-a-customer#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-all-bridge-wallets-for-a-customer#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a bridge wallet id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a bridge wallet right AFTER the specified bridge wallet id on the bridge wallet timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that bridge wallets older than the specified bridge wallet id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-all-bridge-wallets-for-a-customer#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a bridge wallet id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a bridge wallet right BEFORE the specified bridge wallet id on the bridge wallet timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that bridge wallets newer than the specified bridge wallet id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

#### Response

200

application/json

List of Bridge Wallets

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-all-bridge-wallets-for-a-customer#response-count)

count

integer

required

total number of items in data

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-all-bridge-wallets-for-a-customer#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

Get total balances of all Bridge Wallets

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)

Get total balances of all Bridge Wallets

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/wallets/total_balances \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

TotalBalancesFound

    [\
      {\
        "balance": "100.25",\
        "currency": "usdb",\
        "chain": "solana",\
        "contract_address": "ENL66PGy8d8j5KNqLtCcg4uidDUac5ibt45wbjH9REzB"\
      }\
    ]

wallets

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-total-balances-of-all-bridge-wallets#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Response

200

application/json

Total balances of all Bridge Wallets

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-total-balances-of-all-bridge-wallets#response-items-balance)

balance

string

required

The total balance of wallets in the given currency ex. "10.95"

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-total-balances-of-all-bridge-wallets#response-items-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

The currency of the total balance

Available options:

`usdb`,

`usdc`,

`usdt`,

`dai`,

`usd`,

`pyusd`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-total-balances-of-all-bridge-wallets#response-items-chain)

chain

enum<string>

required

The chain of the total balance

Available options:

`base`,

`ethereum`,

`solana`,

`tempo`,

`tron`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-total-balances-of-all-bridge-wallets#response-items-contract-address)

contract\_address

string

The contract address of the currency, or null if it is a native currency

# Get transaction history for a Bridge Wallet - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-transaction-history-for-a-bridge-wallet#content-area)

Bridge Wallets

Get transaction history for a Bridge Wallet

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Get transaction history for a Bridge Wallet

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/wallets/{bridgeWalletID}/history \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

Example

    {
      "count": 123,
      "data": [\
        {\
          "amount": "<string>",\
          "developer_fee": "<string>",\
          "created_at": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",\
          "updated_at": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",\
          "customer_id": "<string>",\
          "source": {\
            "payment_rail": "ach",\
            "currency": "usdb"\
          },\
          "destination": {\
            "payment_rail": "ach",\
            "currency": "usdb"\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }

GET

/

wallets

/

{bridgeWalletID}

/

history

Try it

Get transaction history for a Bridge Wallet

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/wallets/{bridgeWalletID}/history \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

Example

    {
      "count": 123,
      "data": [\
        {\
          "amount": "<string>",\
          "developer_fee": "<string>",\
          "created_at": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",\
          "updated_at": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z",\
          "customer_id": "<string>",\
          "source": {\
            "payment_rail": "ach",\
            "currency": "usdb"\
          },\
          "destination": {\
            "payment_rail": "ach",\
            "currency": "usdb"\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-transaction-history-for-a-bridge-wallet#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-transaction-history-for-a-bridge-wallet#parameter-bridge-wallet-id)

bridgeWalletID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-transaction-history-for-a-bridge-wallet#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-transaction-history-for-a-bridge-wallet#parameter-updated-after-ms)

updated\_after\_ms

integer

This is a unix timestamp in milliseconds. If this is specified, objects updated AFTER the specified timestamp will be returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-transaction-history-for-a-bridge-wallet#parameter-updated-before-ms)

updated\_before\_ms

integer

This is a unix timestamp in milliseconds. If this is specified, objects updated BEFORE the specified timestamp will be returned

#### Response

200

application/json

List of transactions for this Bridge Wallet

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-transaction-history-for-a-bridge-wallet#response-count)

count

integer

required

total number of items in data

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-transaction-history-for-a-bridge-wallet#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

*   Click the link above.
*   Fork the collection into your Postman workspace.
*   Set up your API key and environment variables.
*   Start making requests!

Crypto Return Policies

Update an existing crypto return policy

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Update an existing crypto return policy

cURL

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/crypto_return_policies/{policyID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "refund_destination_address": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_blockchain_memo": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_chain": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_currency": "<string>",
      "strategy": "<string>"
    }
    '

200

Example

{ "id": "<string>", "developer\_id": "<string>", "refund\_destination\_address": "<string>", "refund\_destination\_blockchain\_memo": "<string>", "refund\_destination\_chain": "<string>", "refund\_destination\_currency": "<string>", "strategy": "<string>" }

PUT

/

crypto\_return\_policies

/

{policyID}

Try it

Update an existing crypto return policy

cURL

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/crypto_return_policies/{policyID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "refund_destination_address": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_blockchain_memo": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_chain": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_currency": "<string>",
      "strategy": "<string>"
    }
    '

200

Example

{ "id": "<string>", "developer\_id": "<string>", "refund\_destination\_address": "<string>", "refund\_destination\_blockchain\_memo": "<string>", "refund\_destination\_chain": "<string>", "refund\_destination\_currency": "<string>", "strategy": "<string>" }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#parameter-policy-id)

policyID

string

required

#### Body

application/json

Crypto return policy object to be updated

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#body-refund-destination-address)

refund\_destination\_address

string

The address to which the refund will be sent. Required if the strategy is `static_address`, but must be unset if the strategy is `refund_to_sender`.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#body-refund-destination-blockchain-memo)

refund\_destination\_blockchain\_memo

string

The memo to include with the refund transaction. Must be unset if the strategy is `refund_to_sender`.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#body-refund-destination-chain)

refund\_destination\_chain

string

The blockchain on which the refund will be sent. Required if the strategy is `static_address`, but must be unset if the strategy is `refund_to_sender`.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#body-refund-destination-currency)

refund\_destination\_currency

string

The currency to which the refund will be sent. Required if the strategy is `static_address`, but must be unset if the strategy is `refund_to_sender`.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#body-strategy)

strategy

string

The strategy to use for the refund. Can be `refund_to_sender` or `static_address`. We only support multiple policies for `static_address`; different strategies cannot have multiple policies. If multiple `static_address` policies exist, the policy that matches both the currency and chain will be used first. If no such policy is found, the policy that matches only the currency will be used instead.

#### Response

200

application/json

Crypto return policy updated

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#response-id)

id

string

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#response-developer-id)

developer\_id

string

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#response-refund-destination-address)

refund\_destination\_address

string

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#response-refund-destination-blockchain-memo)

refund\_destination\_blockchain\_memo

string

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#response-refund-destination-chain)

refund\_destination\_chain

string

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#response-refund-destination-currency)

refund\_destination\_currency

string

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/crypto-return-policies/update-an-existing-crypto-return-policy#response-strategy)

strategy

string

# Authentication - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Authentication

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Bridge uses API keys to authenticate your requests. You can generate them from the [dashboard](http://dashboard.bridge.xyz/app/keys)
 . **⚠️ API keys are shown only once** at the time of creation. Be sure to copy and store them securely — they cannot be retrieved later.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction#-how-authentication-works)

🔑 How Authentication Works

*   Pass your API key in the Api-Key header using HTTP Basic Auth.
*   No username or password is required — just the API key.
*   All requests must be made over HTTPS; requests over plain HTTP are rejected.
*   Invalid or missing keys will return a 401 Unauthorized.

> ❗️ Keep your API keys secure. They grant full access to your account and should never be shared publicly or within internal tools like Slack or dashboards.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction#sandbox-environment)

Sandbox Environment

*   In the sandbox, API keys are scoped to individual developer accounts.
*   Keys generated in sandbox are not visible to teammates, even if production keys are shared across the org.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction#example-request)

Example Request

    curl --location --request GET 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers' \
    --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
    --header 'Api-Key: <your-api-key>'

YesNo

Crypto Return Policies

Create a new crypto return policy

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Create a new crypto return policy

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/crypto_return_policies \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "refund_destination_address": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_blockchain_memo": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_chain": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_currency": "<string>",
      "strategy": "<string>"
    }
    '

201

Example

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "developer_id": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_address": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_blockchain_memo": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_chain": "<string>",
      "refund_destination_currency": "<string>",
      "strategy": "<string>"
    }

# Idempotency - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/idempotence#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Idempotency

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/idempotence#idempotency)

Idempotency

All `POST` APIs in Bridge require [idempotency](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Glossary/Idempotent)
 to guarantee safe retries and prevent duplicate operations. You must include an `Idempotency-Key` header with a unique value for each request. This ensures that if a request is retried (due to network errors, client timeouts, or unexpected failures), Bridge can detect the duplication and return the same response, without performing the operation again.

> Do not include an Idempotency-Key with GET, PUT, PATCH, or DELETE requests. These methods are naturally idempotent and do not require this header.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/idempotence#how-it-works)

How It Works

*   Include a unique Idempotency-Key (typically a UUID) in the request header of every POST.
*   Bridge guarantees idempotent behavior for 24 hours after the initial request. During this window, any subsequent request with the same Idempotency-Key will return the original response — with no side effects or duplicated operations.
    *   For example, if a request to create a Customer or a Transfer fails or times out, you can safely retry it using the same key to ensure that only one object is ever created.
*   After the 24-hour window expires, reusing the same Idempotency-Key will result in a 422 Unprocessable Entity error.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/idempotence#best-practices)

Best Practices

*   Use a UUID for each new request.
*   Store the UUID in your database to track request state.
*   Reuse the same UUID when retrying a failed request.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/idempotence#example)

Example

    curl --location --request POST 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v1/customers' \
    --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
    --header 'Api-Key: <your-api-key>' \
    --header 'Idempotency-Key: <generated-uuid>' \
    --data-raw '{
      "first_name": "John",
      "last_name": "Doe",
      "email": "johndoe@johndoe.com",
      "address": {
        "street_line_1": "123 Washington St",
        "street_line_2": "Apt 2F",
        "city": "New York",
        "state": "NY",
        "postal_code": "10001",
        "country": "USA"
      },
      "birth_date": "1989-09-09",
      "tax_identification_number": "111-11-1111"
    }'

Update the configured fees

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/developer/fees \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "default_liquidation_address_fee_percent": "0.5"
    }
    '

200

SuccessfulResponse

    {
      "$ref": "#/components/examples/SuccessfulDeveloperFeesUpdateResponse"
    }

#### Body

application/json

The default fee percent that will be applied to all your Liquidation Addresses. The value is a base 100 percentage, i.e. 10.2% is 10.2 in the API.

default\_liquidation\_address\_fee\_percent

string<float>

required

The default fee percent that will be applied to all your Liquidation Addresses. The value is a base 100 percentage, i.e. 10.2% is "10.2" in the API.

Example:

`"0.5"`

200

application/json

The configured fees have been updated for your developer account.

#### Response

200

application/json

Successful fiat payout configuration response

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/fiat-payout-configuration/get-the-fiat-payout-configuration-for-a-customer#response-fiat-payout-configuration)

fiat\_payout\_configuration

object

required

A nested hash structure representing the fiat payout configuration. The top-level keys are currency codes. Each currency maps to a hash where keys are payment rail codes and values are payout names.

Show child attributes

Example:

    {  "usd": { "wire": "developer", "ach": "bridge" },  "eur": { "sepa": "bridge" },  "brl": { "pix": "payment_provider" },  "mxn": { "spei": "payment_provider" }}

YesNo

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a funds request id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a funds request right AFTER the specified id on the timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that funds request older than the specified funds request id will be returned (shouldn't be set if `ending_before` is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a funds request id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a funds request right BEFORE the specified id on the timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that funds request newer than the specified funds request id will be returned (shouldn't be set if `starting_after` is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#parameter-customer-id)

customer\_id

string

If specified, results will be filtered to the given customer\_id only

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#parameter-fraud)

fraud

boolean

If this is specified as either "true" or "false", then only fraudulent or non-fraudulent entries will be returned, respectively

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#parameter-notice-date-starting-on)

notice\_date\_starting\_on

string

A date in the format YYYY-MM-DD. If specified, then only entries with a notice date on or after the provided date, inclusive, will be returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#parameter-notice-date-ending-on)

notice\_date\_ending\_on

string

A date in the format YYYY-MM-DD. If specified, then only entries with a notice date on or before the provided date, inclusive, will be returned

#### Response

200 - application/json

List of funds requests

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#response-count)

count

integer

required

The number of items returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/funds-requests/get-all-funds-requests#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

# Bridge API Pagination Guide - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Bridge API Pagination Guide

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

On this page

*   [Endpoint shape](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#endpoint-shape)
    
*   [Query parameters](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#query-parameters)
    
*   [Response shape](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#response-shape)
    
*   [cURL examples](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#curl-examples)
    
*   [1) Fetch the first page (newest first)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#1-fetch-the-first-page-newest-first)
    
*   [2) Get the next page of older items](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#2-get-the-next-page-of-older-items)
    
*   [3) Fetch newer items since a known id](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#3-fetch-newer-items-since-a-known-id)
    
*   [Practical patterns](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#practical-patterns)
    
*   [Backfill all historical items (older direction)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#backfill-all-historical-items-older-direction)
    
*   [Periodically check for new items (newer direction)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#periodically-check-for-new-items-newer-direction)
    
*   [Boundary behavior](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#boundary-behavior)
    
*   [Tips and best practices](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#tips-and-best-practices)
    
*   [Minimal JavaScript examples](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#minimal-javascript-examples)
    
*   [Backfill older pages](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#backfill-older-pages)
    
*   [Poll for newer items since a known id](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#poll-for-newer-items-since-a-known-id)
    
*   [Summary](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#summary)
    

Most list endpoints return results in reverse chronological order (newest to oldest) and support stable, cursor-based pagination with `starting_after` and `ending_before`.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#endpoint-shape)

**Endpoint shape**
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Base URL: [**https://api.bridge.xyz**](https://api.bridge.xyz/)
    
*   Typical list endpoint pattern: GET /v0/
*   Default order: newest → oldest (unless an endpoint specifies otherwise)
*   Page size: controlled by `limit` (maximum 100)
*   Pagination: cursor-based using item `id` values

Authentication: send your API key in the `Api-Key` header. Security note: do not hardcode live keys in source or docs; use environment variables.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#query-parameters)

**Query parameters**
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `limit`
    *   Description: number of items to return
    *   Range: 1–100
    *   Tip: set explicitly (e.g., `limit=50`) for predictable pagination
*   `starting_after`
    *   Description: fetches items that come after the given id in the default ordering, i.e., older items
    *   How to use: pass the last item’s id from your current page to get the next page of older results
*   `ending_before`
    *   Description: fetches items that come before the given id in the default ordering, i.e., newer items
    *   How to use: pass the first item’s id from a known page to retrieve any items that are newer than it

Use only one of `starting_after` or `ending_before` per request.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#response-shape)

**Response shape**
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   data: array of resource objects (0 to `limit` items)
*   count: number of items in this page (if provided by the endpoint)
*   Stop condition: when `data` is empty, there are no more items in that direction

Note: Field names inside `data` vary by resource. All paginable resources include an `id` used as the cursor.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#curl-examples)

**cURL examples**
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use an environment variable for your API key:

*   macOS/Linux: export BRIDGE\_API\_KEY=“sk\_live\_…”
*   Windows PowerShell: $env:BRIDGE\_API\_KEY = “sk\_live\_…”

Replace with the list endpoint you’re using (e.g., transactions, payouts, etc.).

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#1-fetch-the-first-page-newest-first)

**1) Fetch the first page (newest first)**

This returns the newest 3 items:

    curl --location 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/{resource}?limit=3' \
      --header 'Accept: application/json' \
      --header "Api-Key: $BRIDGE_API_KEY"
    

Take note of:

*   First item’s id: newest on this page
*   Last item’s id: oldest on this page

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#2-get-the-next-page-of-older-items)

**2) Get the next page of older items**

Use `starting_after` with the last id from the previous page:

    curl --location 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/{resource}?limit=3&starting_after={LAST_ID_FROM_PREVIOUS_PAGE}' \
      --header 'Accept: application/json' \
      --header "Api-Key: $BRIDGE_API_KEY"
    

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#3-fetch-newer-items-since-a-known-id)

**3) Fetch newer items since a known id**

If your last run’s first item id was , use `ending_before` to get any newer items:

    curl --location 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/{resource}?ending_before={FIRST_ID_YOU_SAW}' \
      --header 'Accept: application/json' \
      --header "Api-Key: $BRIDGE_API_KEY"
    

If there are new items, they’ll be returned; otherwise you may see an empty page.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#practical-patterns)

**Practical patterns**
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#backfill-all-historical-items-older-direction)

**Backfill all historical items (older direction)**

1.  Request with your chosen `limit` (e.g., 100).
2.  Process the page.
3.  Save the last id from the page (the oldest in this batch).
4.  Repeat with `starting_after=<last_id>` until `data` is empty.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#periodically-check-for-new-items-newer-direction)

**Periodically check for new items (newer direction)**

1.  Save the first id from your last successful fetch (the newest you’ve seen).
2.  Request with `ending_before=<that_first_id>`.
3.  If `data` is non-empty, process the new items and update your saved first id to the newest id returned.
4.  If empty, nothing new is available.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#boundary-behavior)

**Boundary behavior**

*   Reached oldest items: using `starting_after` eventually returns `data: []`.
*   No newer items: using `ending_before` may return `data: []`.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#tips-and-best-practices)

**Tips and best practices**
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Treat item ids as stable cursors; always use the first and last ids from each page for the next request.
*   Don’t combine `starting_after` and `ending_before` in the same call.
*   Stick to a consistent `limit` for predictable throughput; max is 100.
*   Expect partial pages near the ends (fewer than `limit` items).
*   If you need to process items oldest-to-newest, reverse the page locally after fetching.
*   When running concurrent pagination and ingestion, de-duplicate by `id` in your datastore.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#minimal-javascript-examples)

**Minimal JavaScript examples**
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Assume a helper fetchFn(path) that does authenticated fetches relative to [**https://api.bridge.xyz**](https://api.bridge.xyz/)
.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#backfill-older-pages)

**Backfill older pages**

    // Fetch older pages until no more items are returned.
    const backfillAll = async (fetchFn) => {
      let startingAfter = null;
      const pageSize = 100;
    
      while (true) {
        const qs = new URLSearchParams({ limit: String(pageSize) });
        if (startingAfter) qs.set("starting_after", startingAfter);
    
        const res = await fetchFn(`/v0/{resource}?${qs.toString()}`);
        const { data = [] } = await res.json();
    
        if (data.length === 0) break;
    
        // Process items (newest → oldest on this page)
        // ...
    
        // Next cursor: last id (oldest on this page)
        startingAfter = data[data.length - 1].id;
      }
    };
    

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#poll-for-newer-items-since-a-known-id)

**Poll for newer items since a known id**

    // Fetch any items newer than `firstSeenId`.
    // Returns the updated newest id to store for next poll.
    const fetchNewerSince = async (fetchFn, firstSeenId) => {
      const qs = new URLSearchParams({ ending_before: firstSeenId });
      const res = await fetchFn(`/v0/{resource}?${qs.toString()}`);
      const { data = [] } = await res.json();
    
      if (data.length > 0) {
        // Items returned are newest → oldest within the page.
        // Update the cursor to the newest id we now know about.
        return data[0].id;
      }
      return firstSeenId;
    };
    

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/pagination#summary)

**Summary**
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Results are newest → oldest by default.
*   Use `starting_after=<last_id>` to go older.
*   Use `ending_before=<first_id>` to fetch items newer than a known id.
*   Control page size with `limit` (max 100).
*   Stop when `data` is empty in the direction you’re traversing.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Get all Bridge Wallets](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/bridge-wallets/get-all-bridge-wallets)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

*   ach: `^(?!\s*$)[\x20-\x7E]*$`
*   wire: ``^[ \w!"#$%&'()+,\-./:;<=>?@\\_`~]*$``

Bank name of the account (e.g. "Chase")

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/get-the-configured-fee-external-account#response-account-owner-type)

account\_owner\_type

enum<string>

The type of the account ownership. Required when the `account_type` is `iban`. For `individual` ownership, `first_name` and `last_name` are required. For `business` ownership, `business_name` is required.

Available options:

`individual`,

`business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/get-the-configured-fee-external-account#response-first-name)

first\_name

string

First name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/get-the-configured-fee-external-account#response-last-name)

last\_name

string

Last name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/get-the-configured-fee-external-account#response-business-name)

business\_name

string

Business name of the business account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/get-the-configured-fee-external-account#response-deactivation-reason)

deactivation\_reason

enum<string>

Reason for deactivation when this External Account is inactive

Available options:

`plaid_item_error`,

`deactivated_due_to_bounceback`,

`deleted_by_developer`,

`requested_by_developer`,

`invalid_account_number`,

`invalid_bank_validation`,

`rejected_by_bank_provider`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/get-the-configured-fee-external-account#response-deactivation-details)

deactivation\_details

string

Additional details about the deactivation when this External Account is inactive

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/get-the-configured-fee-external-account#response-beneficiary-address-valid)

beneficiary\_address\_valid

boolean

Whether the beneficiary address is valid. A valid beneficiary address is required for all US External Accounts

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/get-the-configured-fee-external-account#response-last-4)

last\_4

string

deprecated

Last 4 digits of the bank account number. This field is getting deprecated in favor of the `account.last_4` field

Minimum string length: `1`

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Update the configured fees](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/update-the-configured-fees)
[Configure a fee External Account](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/get-all-kyc-links#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/get-all-kyc-links#parameter-customer-id)

customer\_id

string

If included, filters to KYC links for the customer with the given id

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/get-all-kyc-links#parameter-email)

email

string

If included, filters to KYC links for the customer with the given email

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/get-all-kyc-links#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a customer id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a customer right AFTER the specified customer id on the customer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that customers older than the specified customer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/get-all-kyc-links#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a customer id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a customer right BEFORE the specified customer id on the customer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that customers newer than the specified customer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/get-all-kyc-links#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

#### Response

200

application/json

Successful KYC links status response

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/get-all-kyc-links#response-count)

count

integer

required

total number of items in data

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/get-all-kyc-links#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

Fiat Payout Configuration

Update the fiat payout configuration for a customer

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Update the fiat payout configuration for a customer

cURL

    curl --request PATCH \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/fiat_payout_configuration \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "usd": {
        "wire": "customer"
      }
    }
    '

200

SuccessfulPatchFiatPayoutConfigurationResponse

    {
      "fiat_payout_configuration": {
        "usd": {
          "wire": "customer",
          "ach": "bridge"
        },
        "eur": {
          "sepa": "bridge"
        },
        "brl": {
          "pix": "payment_provider"
        },
        "mxn": {
          "spei": "payment_provider"
        }
      }
    }

PATCH

/

customers

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/fiat-payout-configuration/update-the-fiat-payout-configuration-for-a-customer#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/fiat-payout-configuration/update-the-fiat-payout-configuration-for-a-customer#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Body

application/json

Fiat payout configuration to update

Input payload for updating a customer's fiat payout configuration

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/fiat-payout-configuration/update-the-fiat-payout-configuration-for-a-customer#body-fiat-payout-configuration)

fiat\_payout\_configuration

object

required

A nested hash structure representing the fiat payout configuration. The top-level keys are currency codes. Each currency maps to a hash where keys are payment rail codes and values are payout names.

Show child attributes

Example:

    {  "usd": { "wire": "developer", "ach": "bridge" },  "eur": { "sepa": "bridge" },  "brl": { "pix": "payment_provider" },  "mxn": { "spei": "payment_provider" }}

#### Response

200

application/json

Successful fiat payout configuration update response

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/fiat-payout-configuration/update-the-fiat-payout-configuration-for-a-customer#response-fiat-payout-configuration)

fiat\_payout\_configuration

object

required

A nested hash structure representing the fiat payout configuration. The top-level keys are currency codes. Each currency maps to a hash where keys are payment rail codes and values are payout names.

Show child attributes

Example:

    {  "usd": { "wire": "developer", "ach": "bridge" },  "eur": { "sepa": "bridge" },  "brl": { "pix": "payment_provider" },  "mxn": { "spei": "payment_provider" }}

Exchange Plaid public token for an access token

cURL

      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/plaid_exchange_public_token/{link_token} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "public_token": "<string>"
    }
    '

201

PlaidExchangePublicTokenSuccessResponse

    {
      "message": "Successfully exchanged public token for access token"
    }

# Generate the Links needs to complete KYC for an individual or business - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

KYC Links

Generate the Links needs to complete KYC for an individual or business

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Generate the Links needs to complete KYC for an individual or business

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/kyc_links \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "email": "<string>",
      "type": "individual",
      "full_name": "<string>",
      "endorsements": [\
        "base"\
      ],
      "redirect_uri": "<string>",
      "transliterated_first_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_middle_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_last_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_business_legal_name": "<string>"
    }
    '

200

SuccessfulLiquidationAddressCreateResponse

    {
      "id": "kyc_link_123",
      "full_name": "John Doe",
      "email": "johndoe@johndoe.com",
      "type": "individual",
      "kyc_link": "www.kyclink.com/blah",
      "tos_link": "www.toslink.com/blah",
      "kyc_status": "not_started",
      "tos_status": "pending",
      "customer_id": "cust_123"
    }

POST

/

kyc\_links

      "transliterated_first_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_middle_name": "<string>",
