#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Headers

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#parameter-idempotency-key)

Idempotency-Key

string

required

#### Body

application/json

Information about the customer to create KYC Links for

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-email)

email

string

required

Email of the customer

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-type)

type

enum<string>

required

Type of the customer (individual vs. business)

Available options:

`individual`,

`business`

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-full-name)

full\_name

string

Full name of the customer, for a business, this would be the business entity's legal name

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-endorsements)

endorsements

enum<string>\[\]

List of endorsements to request for the generated KYC link. For example, `sepa` endorsement could be requested to allow an `individual` customer to submit `proof-of-address` documents in the KYC flow.

The type of endorsement.

Available options:

`base`,

`cards`,

`cop`,

`faster_payments`,

`pix`,

`sepa`,

`spei`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-redirect-uri)

redirect\_uri

string

The location where the customer should be redirected after completing the KYC flow. Must be in the form of http:// or https://.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-transliterated-first-name)

transliterated\_first\_name

string

Required when the `full_name` of an individual includes any non Latin-1 characters. Acceptable characters - Latin-1 Unicode Character Range: À-ÖØ-ßà-öø-ÿ; Standard Unicode Character Range: -~

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-transliterated-middle-name)

transliterated\_middle\_name

string

Required when the `full_name` of an individual includes any non Latin-1 characters and the individual has a middle name. Acceptable characters - Latin-1 Unicode Character Range: À-ÖØ-ßà-öø-ÿ; Standard Unicode Character Range: -~

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-transliterated-last-name)

transliterated\_last\_name

string

Required when the `full_name` of an individual includes any non Latin-1 characters. Acceptable characters - Latin-1 Unicode Character Range: À-ÖØ-ßà-öø-ÿ; Standard Unicode Character Range: -~

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/kyc-links/generate-the-links-needs-to-complete-kyc-for-an-individual-or-business#body-transliterated-business-legal-name)

transliterated\_business\_legal\_name

string

Required if the `full_name` of a business includes any non Latin-1 characters. Acceptable characters - Latin-1 Unicode Character Range: À-ÖØ-ßà-öø-ÿ; Standard Unicode Character Range: -~

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

Build with Bridge.
==================

Bridge provides modern payments infrastructure to move money with stablecoins and fiat rails, custody funds via wallets, issue your own stablecoin, and provision globally accepted cards — at the speed and scale of the internet.

[Get started →](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)

Quickstart guides
-----------------

Create a virtual account
------------------------

Use a virtual account to accept deposits in USD, EUR, GBP, MXN, and more with a unique account & routing number.

Make payments
-------------

Easily create onramps, offramps, and crypto to crypto transfers using our orchestration APIs.

Provision cards
---------------

Provision a card backed by stablecoins and spend anywhere in the world.

Create wallets
--------------

Custody funds in a wallet. Use it to send, receive, or hold stablecoins.

Issue stablecoins
-----------------

Issue your own stablecoin and start earning yield.

Resources
---------

Contact support
---------------

Reach out to our team for help with integration or technical issues.

Request sales
-------------

Click here to request a demo!

Demo
----

Watch our interactive demo to see Bridge in action.

# Configure a fee External Account - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Developers

Configure a fee External Account

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Configure a fee External Account

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/developer/fee_external_account \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "currency": "usd",
      "bank_name": "Wells Fargo",
      "account_owner_name": "John Doe",
      "account_type": "us",
      "account": {
        "account_number": "1210002481111",
        "routing_number": "121000248",
        "checking_or_savings": "checking"
      },
      "address": {
        "street_line_1": "123 Main St",
        "city": "San Francisco",
        "state": "CA",
        "postal_code": "94102",
        "country": "USA"
      }
    }
    '

201

SuccessfulFeeExternalAccountResponse

    {
      "id": "fea_123",
      "account_type": "us",
      "currency": "usd",
      "account_owner_name": "John Doe",
      "bank_name": "Wells Fargo",
      "last_4": "1111",
      "active": true,
      "beneficiary_address_valid": true,
      "account": {
        "last_4": "1111",
        "routing_number": "121000248",
        "checking_or_savings": "checking"
      },
      "created_at": "2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
      "updated_at": "2020-01-02T00:00:00.000Z"
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Headers

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#parameter-idempotency-key)

Idempotency-Key

string

required

#### Body

application/json

New External Account object to be created

Request body for creating a fee external account. Fee external accounts must use USD currency.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-account-owner-name)

account\_owner\_name

string

required

Owner of the account Bank Account (e.g. "John Doe"). For ach or wire transfers, this field must be at least 3 characters, at most 35 characters, and follow either of the following regex patterns:

*   ach: `^(?!\s*$)[\x20-\x7E]*$`
*   wire: ``^[ \w!"#$%&'()+,\-./:;<=>?@\\_`~]*$``

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-account-type)

account\_type

enum<string>

required

Type of the bank account.

Available options:

`us`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

Currency associated with the bank account. Must be `usd` for US accounts.

Available options:

`usd`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-account)

account

us · object

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-bank-name)

bank\_name

string

Bank name of the account (e.g. "Chase")

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-account-owner-type)

account\_owner\_type

enum<string>

The type of the account ownership. Required when the `account_type` is `iban`. For `individual` ownership, `first_name` and `last_name` are required. For `business` ownership, `business_name` is required.

Available options:

`individual`,

`business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-first-name)

first\_name

string

First name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-last-name)

last\_name

string

Last name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-business-name)

business\_name

string

Business name of the business account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-address)

address

object

Address of the beneficiary of this account. Please ensure the address is valid (Google Maps is good for this). US addresses used to receive wires must include a street number.

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-account-number)

account\_number

string

deprecated

Account number of your bank account. This field is getting deprecated in favor of the `account.account_number` field for US accounts.

Minimum string length: `12`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#body-routing-number)

routing\_number

string

deprecated

Routing number of your bank account. This field is getting deprecated in favor of the `account.routing_number` field for US accounts.

Minimum string length: `9`

#### Response

201

application/json

External Account object created

US bank account using account and routing numbers for ACH or Wire transfers

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-id)

id

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-customer-id)

customer\_id

string

required

The id of the Bridge customer that this External Account belongs to

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-account-owner-name)

account\_owner\_name

string

required

Owner of the account Bank Account (e.g. "John Doe"). For ach or wire transfers, this field must be at least 3 characters, at most 35 characters, and follow either of the following regex patterns:

*   ach: `^(?!\s*$)[\x20-\x7E]*$`
*   wire: ``^[ \w!"#$%&'()+,\-./:;<=>?@\\_`~]*$``

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of creation of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of last update of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-active)

active

boolean

required

Whether or not this External Account is active

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-account-type)

account\_type

enum<string>

required

Type of the bank account.

Available options:

`us`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

Currency associated with the bank account. Must be `usd` for US accounts.

Available options:

`usd`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-account)

account

us · object

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-bank-name)

bank\_name

string

Bank name of the account (e.g. "Chase")

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-account-owner-type)

account\_owner\_type

enum<string>

The type of the account ownership. Required when the `account_type` is `iban`. For `individual` ownership, `first_name` and `last_name` are required. For `business` ownership, `business_name` is required.

Available options:

`individual`,

`business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-first-name)

first\_name

string

First name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-last-name)

last\_name

string

Last name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-business-name)

business\_name

string

Business name of the business account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-deactivation-reason)

deactivation\_reason

enum<string>

Reason for deactivation when this External Account is inactive

Available options:

`plaid_item_error`,

`deactivated_due_to_bounceback`,

`deleted_by_developer`,

`requested_by_developer`,

`invalid_account_number`,

`invalid_bank_validation`,

`rejected_by_bank_provider`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-deactivation-details)

deactivation\_details

string

Additional details about the deactivation when this External Account is inactive

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-beneficiary-address-valid)

beneficiary\_address\_valid

boolean

Whether the beneficiary address is valid. A valid beneficiary address is required for all US External Accounts

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/developers/configure-a-fee-external-account#response-last-4)

last\_4

string

deprecated

Last 4 digits of the bank account number. This field is getting deprecated in favor of the `account.last_4` field

Minimum string length: `1`

Generate a Plaid Link token for a customer

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/plaid_link_requests \

      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>'

201

      "link_token": "plaid_link_token_123",
      "link_token_expires_at": "2023-03-23T03:22:34.086Z",
      "callback_url": "https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/plaid_exchange_public_token/plaid_link_token_123"
    }

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/generate-a-card-account-statement#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

string

required

#### Response

200

application/pdf

The HTTP response that includes a PDF file as an attachment, with the `Content-Type` set to `application/pdf` and the `Content-Disposition` header configured to indicate it is a statement PDF attachment

The response is of type `file`.

# Cards - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/overview#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Provision and make card payments

Cards

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Bridge cards let customers spend stablecoin balances virtually anywhere in the world that accept Visa - with a virtual card, a physical card, or a mobile wallet. Using Bridge APIs, you can seamlessly provision new cards for your customers, manage balances, and more. Bridge cards are:

*   **Multi-market:** Launch a card product in multiple markets with a single integration.
*   **Flexible:** Bridge supports custodial and non-custodial wallets.
*   **Integrated:** Use card issuing with virtual accounts and wallets to build seamless experiences around sending, receiving, storing and spending stablecoins.
*   **Revenue generating:** Generate revenue based on your customers’ card spend. Earn a share of profit earned from the card program.

Refer the [Cards](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/cards/overview/overview)
 section for more in depth details.

YesNo

[Spend wallet balances using a card](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend)

# Geographies - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/geo#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

What we support

Geographies

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/geo#regional-availability)

Regional Availability

Bridge can be used to facilitate payments for customers in most countries not on the OFAC sanctions list.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/geo#united-states-specific-details)

United States Specific Details

Within the United States, we can support your customers (both individuals and businesses) in most states, excluding those with a **principal residential or operating addresses (as applicable)** in New York.  
  
You can now onboard both businesses and individual users from Florida and Louisiana to transact with Bridge. For businesses, these exclusions can be complicated —a few examples below:

*   What we can support:
    *   A business’s registered and operating address is in California, but they bank with Chase in New York City
    *   A business is incorporated in New York but primarily operates out of California (Proof of Address verification required)
*   What we cannot support:
    *   A business’s primary operating address is in New York, and they bank with Wells Fargo in California
    *   A business is incorporated in California but primarily operates their business from within New York

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/geo#europe-specific-details)

Europe Specific Details

For customers in some European countries, we require proof of address. Refer [Proof of Address Requirements](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/customers/compliance/poa)
 for the list of countries.

Get all External Accounts

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/external_accounts \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

ExternalAccountsFound

    {

        }\

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts-1#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts-1#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts-1#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is an external account id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with an external account right AFTER the specified external account id on the external account timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that external accounts older than the specified external account id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts-1#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is an external account id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with an external account right BEFORE the specified external account id on the external account timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that external accounts newer than the specified external account id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

#### Response

200 - application/json

List of External Accounts (the returned list is empty if no External Accounts exist)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts-1#response-data)

data

(ACH/Wire · object | IBAN · object | SWIFT · object | CLABE · object | Pix · object | GB · object | Bre-B · object)\[\]

required

US bank account using account and routing numbers for ACH or Wire transfers

*   ACH/Wire
    
*   IBAN
    
*   SWIFT
    
*   CLABE
    
*   Pix
    
*   GB
    
*   Bre-B
    

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts-1#response-count)

count

integer

total number of items in data

id

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

customer\_id

string

required

The id of the Bridge customer that this External Account belongs to

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account-owner-name)

account\_owner\_name

string

required

Owner of the account Bank Account (e.g. "John Doe"). For ach or wire transfers, this field must be at least 3 characters, at most 35 characters, and follow either of the following regex patterns:

*   ach: `^(?!\s*$)[\x20-\x7E]*$`
*   wire: ``^[ \w!"#$%&'()+,\-./:;<=>?@\\_`~]*$``

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of creation of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of last update of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-active)

active

boolean

required

Whether or not this External Account is active

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account-type)

account\_type

enum<string>

required

Type of the bank account.

Available options:

`us`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

Currency associated with the bank account. Must be `usd` for US accounts.

Available options:

`usd`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account)

account

us · object

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-bank-name)

bank\_name

string

Bank name of the account (e.g. "Chase")

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account-owner-type)

account\_owner\_type

enum<string>

The type of the account ownership. Required when the `account_type` is `iban`. For `individual` ownership, `first_name` and `last_name` are required. For `business` ownership, `business_name` is required.

Available options:

`individual`,

`business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-first-name)

first\_name

string

First name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-last-name)

last\_name

string

Last name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-business-name)

business\_name

string

Business name of the business account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-deactivation-reason)

deactivation\_reason

enum<string>

Reason for deactivation when this External Account is inactive

Available options:

`plaid_item_error`,

`deactivated_due_to_bounceback`,

`deleted_by_developer`,

`requested_by_developer`,

`invalid_account_number`,

`invalid_bank_validation`,

`rejected_by_bank_provider`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-deactivation-details)

deactivation\_details

string

Additional details about the deactivation when this External Account is inactive

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-beneficiary-address-valid)

beneficiary\_address\_valid

boolean

Whether the beneficiary address is valid. A valid beneficiary address is required for all US External Accounts

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-last-4)

last\_4

string

deprecated

Last 4 digits of the bank account number. This field is getting deprecated in favor of the `account.last_4` field

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/reactivate-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account-validation-one-of-0)

account\_validation

object

Present for Pix, SPEI/CLABE, and Bre-B accounts with a successful validation; contains validated owner and bank name.

Show child attributes

Try it

Get all External Accounts

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/external_accounts \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

ExternalAccountsFound

    {
      "data": [\
        {\
          "$ref": "#/components/examples/SuccessfulExternalAccountResponse/value"\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is an external account id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with an external account right AFTER the specified external account id on the external account timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that external accounts older than the specified external account id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is an external account id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with an external account right BEFORE the specified external account id on the external account timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that external accounts newer than the specified external account id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

#### Response

200

application/json

List of External Accounts (the returned list is empty if no External Accounts exist)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts#response-data)

data

(ACH/Wire · object | IBAN · object | SWIFT · object | CLABE · object | Pix · object | GB · object | Bre-B · object)\[\]

required

US bank account using account and routing numbers for ACH or Wire transfers

*   ACH/Wire
    
*   IBAN
    
*   SWIFT
    
*   CLABE
    
*   Pix
    
*   GB
    
*   Bre-B
    

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/get-all-external-accounts#response-count)

count

integer

total number of items in data

This also implies that liquidation address newer than the specified liquidation address id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

id

customer\_id

string

required

The id of the Bridge customer that this External Account belongs to

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-account-owner-name)

account\_owner\_name

string

required

Owner of the account Bank Account (e.g. "John Doe"). For ach or wire transfers, this field must be at least 3 characters, at most 35 characters, and follow either of the following regex patterns:

*   ach: `^(?!\s*$)[\x20-\x7E]*$`
*   wire: ``^[ \w!"#$%&'()+,\-./:;<=>?@\\_`~]*$``

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of creation of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of last update of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-active)

active

boolean

required

Whether or not this External Account is active

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-account-type)

account\_type

enum<string>

required

Type of the bank account.

Available options:

`us`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

Currency associated with the bank account. Must be `usd` for US accounts.

Available options:

`usd`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-account)

account

us · object

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-bank-name)

bank\_name

string

Bank name of the account (e.g. "Chase")

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-account-owner-type)

account\_owner\_type

enum<string>

The type of the account ownership. Required when the `account_type` is `iban`. For `individual` ownership, `first_name` and `last_name` are required. For `business` ownership, `business_name` is required.

Available options:

`individual`,

`business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-first-name)

first\_name

string

First name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-last-name)

last\_name

string

Last name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-business-name)

business\_name

string

Business name of the business account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-deactivation-reason)

deactivation\_reason

enum<string>

Reason for deactivation when this External Account is inactive

Available options:

`plaid_item_error`,

`deactivated_due_to_bounceback`,

`deleted_by_developer`,

`requested_by_developer`,

`invalid_account_number`,

`invalid_bank_validation`,

`rejected_by_bank_provider`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-deactivation-details)

deactivation\_details

string

Additional details about the deactivation when this External Account is inactive

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-beneficiary-address-valid)

beneficiary\_address\_valid

boolean

Whether the beneficiary address is valid. A valid beneficiary address is required for all US External Accounts

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-last-4)

last\_4

string

deprecated

Last 4 digits of the bank account number. This field is getting deprecated in favor of the `account.last_4` field

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/deactivate-a-single-external-account-object#response-one-of-0-account-validation-one-of-0)

account\_validation

object

Present for Pix, SPEI/CLABE, and Bre-B accounts with a successful validation; contains validated owner and bank name.

Show child attributes

Retrieve an External Account object

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)

[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Retrieve an External Account object

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/external_accounts/{externalAccountID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulExternalAccountResponse

    {
      "id": "ea_123",
      "account_type": "us",
      "currency": "usd",
      "customer_id": "cust_123",
      "account_owner_name": "John Doe",
      "bank_name": "Wells Fargo",
      "last_4": "1111",
      "active": true,
      "beneficiary_address_valid": true,
      "account": {
        "last_4": "1111",
        "routing_number": "121000248",
        "checking_or_savings": "checking"
      },
      "created_at": "2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
      "updated_at": "2020-01-02T00:00:00.000Z"
    }

Create a mobile wallet push provisioning request

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Create a mobile wallet push provisioning request

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/card_accounts/{cardAccountID}/create_mobile_wallet_provisioning_request \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "wallet_provider": "apple_pay"
    }
    '

200

Example

    {
      "wallet_provider": "apple_pay",
      "apple_pay": {
        "activation_data": "<string>",
        "encrypted_pass_data": "<string>",
        "ephemeral_public_key": "<string>"
      },
      "google_pay": {
        "opaque_payment_card": "<string>"
      }
    }

# Get drain history of a Liquidation Address - Bridge

Liquidation Addresses

Get drain history of a Liquidation Address

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Get drain history of a Liquidation Address

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/liquidation_addresses/{liquidationAddressID}/drains \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

DrainsToCryptoFound

    {
      "count": 1,
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": "la_123",\
          "amount": "100.25",\
          "customer_id": "cust_123",\
          "liquidation_address_id": "la_456",\
          "currency": "usdc",\
          "state": "funds_received",\
          "created_at": "2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",\
          "updated_at": "2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",\
          "deposit_tx_hash": "0xc13d7905be5c989378a945487cd2a1193627ae606009e28e296d48ddaec66162",\
          "destination": {\
            "payment_rail": "ethereum",\
            "currency": "usdt",\
            "to_address": "0xb794f5ea0ba39494ce839613fffba74279579268"\
          },\
          "destination_tx_hash": "0xdeadbeef",\
          "receipt": {\
            "initial_amount": "100.25",\
            "developer_fee": "0.2",\
            "subtotal_amount": "100.05",\
            "exchange_rate": "1.000000",\
            "converted_amount": "100.05",\
            "outgoing_amount": "100.05",\
            "destination_currency": "usd",\
            "url": "https://dashboard.bridge.xyz/transaction/00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000/receipt/00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }

Get drain history of a Liquidation Address

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/liquidation_addresses/{liquidationAddressID}/drains \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

DrainsToCryptoFound

    {
      "count": 1,
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": "la_123",\
          "amount": "100.25",\
          "customer_id": "cust_123",\
          "liquidation_address_id": "la_456",\
          "currency": "usdc",\
          "state": "funds_received",\
          "created_at": "2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",\
          "updated_at": "2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",\
          "deposit_tx_hash": "0xc13d7905be5c989378a945487cd2a1193627ae606009e28e296d48ddaec66162",\
          "destination": {\
            "payment_rail": "ethereum",\
            "currency": "usdt",\
            "to_address": "0xb794f5ea0ba39494ce839613fffba74279579268"\
          },\
          "destination_tx_hash": "0xdeadbeef",\
          "receipt": {\
            "initial_amount": "100.25",\
            "developer_fee": "0.2",\
            "subtotal_amount": "100.05",\
            "exchange_rate": "1.000000",\
            "converted_amount": "100.05",\
            "outgoing_amount": "100.05",\
            "destination_currency": "usd",\
            "url": "https://dashboard.bridge.xyz/transaction/00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000/receipt/00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#parameter-liquidation-address-id)

liquidationAddressID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a drain id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a drain right AFTER the specified drain id on the drain timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that drains older than the specified drain id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a drain id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a drain right BEFORE the specified drain id on the drain timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that drains newer than the specified drain id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#parameter-updated-after-ms)

updated\_after\_ms

integer

This is a unix timestamp in milliseconds. If this is specified, objects updated AFTER the specified timestamp will be returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#parameter-updated-before-ms)

updated\_before\_ms

integer

This is a unix timestamp in milliseconds. If this is specified, objects updated BEFORE the specified timestamp will be returned

#### Response

200

application/json

List of drains (the returned list is empty if none found)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-drain-history-of-a-liquidation-address#response-data)

data

object

Show child attributes

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Prefunded Accounts

Get funding history of a Prefunded Account

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Get funding history of a Prefunded Account

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/prefunded_accounts/{prefundedAccountID}/history \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulCustomerResponse

    {
      "count": 1,
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": "abced012-4cdd-460c-9da3-34f7321bfa3f",\
          "amount": "500.00",\
          "available_balance": "1300.31",\
          "currency": "usd",\
          "name": "my_account",\
          "type": "funding",\
          "created_at": "2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"\
        }\
      ]
    }

GET

/

prefunded\_accounts

/

{prefundedAccountID}

/

history

Try it

Get funding history of a Prefunded Account

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/prefunded_accounts/{prefundedAccountID}/history \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulCustomerResponse

    {
      "count": 1,
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": "abced012-4cdd-460c-9da3-34f7321bfa3f",\
          "amount": "500.00",\
          "available_balance": "1300.31",\
          "currency": "usd",\
          "name": "my_account",\
          "type": "funding",\
          "created_at": "2020-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"\
        }\
      ]
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#parameter-prefunded-account-id)

prefundedAccountID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a prefunded event id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with an event right AFTER the specified event id on the event timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that events older than the specified event id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a prefunded event id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with an event right BEFORE the specified event id on the event timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that events newer than the specified event id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

#### Response

200

application/json

Successful Prefunded Account object response

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-id)

id

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-amount)

amount

string

required

Amount of the transaction, represented as a dollar denominated string. Examples include "100.25", "0.1", "1.234567", "1.01" etc.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-available-balance)

available\_balance

string

required

Amount available for spending, represented as a dollar denominated string. Examples include "100.25", "0.1", "1.234567", "1.01" etc.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

currency associated with the bank account.

Available options:

`usd`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-name)

name

string

required

Serialized name of the account.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-type)

type

enum<string>

required

The type of the transaction.

Available options:

`funding`,

`refunded transfer`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of creation of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-withdrawal-id)

withdrawal\_id

string

The ID of the transfer which created this event. Exclusive with deposit\_id.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/prefunded-accounts/get-funding-history-of-a-prefunded-account#response-deposit-id)

deposit\_id

string

The ID of the transfer which created this event. Exclusive with withdrawal\_id.

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/liquidation-address-activity-across-all-customers#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/liquidation-address-activity-across-all-customers#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a drain id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a drain right AFTER the specified drain id on the drain timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that drains older than the specified drain id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/liquidation-address-activity-across-all-customers#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a drain id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a drain right BEFORE the specified drain id on the drain timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that drains newer than the specified drain id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/liquidation-address-activity-across-all-customers#parameter-updated-after-ms)

updated\_after\_ms

integer

This is a unix timestamp in milliseconds. If this is specified, objects updated AFTER the specified timestamp will be returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/liquidation-address-activity-across-all-customers#parameter-updated-before-ms)

updated\_before\_ms

integer

This is a unix timestamp in milliseconds. If this is specified, objects updated BEFORE the specified timestamp will be returned

200

application/json

integer

required

object\[\]

Get a Liquidation Address

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/liquidation_addresses/{liquidationAddressID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulLiquidationAddressGetResponse

    {
      "id": "la_123",
      "chain": "ethereum",
      "customer_id": "cust_123",
      "external_account_id": "ext_123",
      "address": "0x4d0280da2f2fDA5103914bCc5aad114743152A9c",
      "currency": "usdc",
      "destination_payment_rail": "wire",
      "destination_currency": "usd",
      "destination_wire_message": "a wire message",
      "state": "active",
      "created_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",
      "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"
    }

      "customer_id": "cust_123",

      "destination_currency": "usd",

      "state": "active",
      "created_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",
      "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"
    }

200

application/json

A Liquidation Address object response

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-id)

id

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

currency

enum<string>

required

`usdb`,

`usdc`,

`usdt`,

`dai`,

customer\_id

string

required

The ID of the customer who owns this liquidation address

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-external-account-id)

external\_account\_id

string

required

External bank account to which Bridge will send the funds. The currency associated with the External Account must match the destination currency.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-payment-rail)

destination\_payment\_rail

enum<string>

required

The payment rail that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer.

Available options:

`ach`,

`wire`,

`ach_push`,

`ach_same_day`,

`arbitrum`,

`avalanche_c_chain`,

`base`,

`bre_b`,

`celo`,

`ethereum`,

`faster_payments`,

`fiat_deposit_return`,

`optimism`,

`pix`,

`polygon`,

`sepa`,

`solana`,

`spei`,

`stellar`,

`swift`,

`tempo`,

`tron`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-currency)

destination\_currency

enum<string>

required

The currency that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer.

Available options:

`brl`,

`cop`,

`dai`,

`eur`,

`eurc`,

`gbp`,

`mxn`,

`pyusd`,

`usd`,

`usdb`,

`usdc`,

`usdt`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-address)

address

string

required

The crypto wallet address the customer will send funds to in order to initiate the payment processing

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of creation of the Liquidation Address

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of last update of the Liquidation Address

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-prefunded-account-id)

prefunded\_account\_id

string

The developer's prefunded account to which Bridge will send the funds.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-custom-developer-fee-percent-one-of-0)

custom\_developer\_fee\_percent

string<number> | null

The developer fee percent that will be applied to this Liquidation Address or null to use the default fee. The value is a base 100 percentage, i.e. 10.2% is 10.2 in the API.

Example:

`"0.1"`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-global-developer-fee-percent)

global\_developer\_fee\_percent

object

The developer fee percent that will be default applied to all Liquidation Addresses.

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-wire-message)

destination\_wire\_message

string

A message to be sent with a wire transfer.

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-sepa-reference)

destination\_sepa\_reference

string

A reference message to be sent with a SEPA transaction. We recommend you set a unique value to help you and your customers track payments end to end. It must be from 6 to 140 characters. The allowed characters are `a-z`, `A-Z`, `0-9`, spaces, ampersand (`&`), hyphen (`-`), full stop (`.`), and solidus (`/`). If not populated, the default value is "Payment via Bridge {unique\_token}".

Required string length: `6 - 140`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-spei-reference)

destination\_spei\_reference

string

A payment reference message or remittance information to be included in a SPEI transaction. The allowed characters are alphanumeric `a-z`, `A-Z`, `0-9`, and space

Required string length: `1 - 40`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-ach-reference)

destination\_ach\_reference

string

A reference message to be sent with an ACH transaction. It can be at most 10 characters, A-Z, a-z, 0-9, and spaces.

Required string length: `1 - 10`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-address)

destination\_address

string

The crypto wallet address that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-blockchain-memo)

destination\_blockchain\_memo

string

The memo to include in the transaction, for blockchains that support memos only

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-return-address)

return\_address

string

The crypto wallet address that Bridge will use to return funds to the customer in case of a failed transaction. This address must be on the same chain specified for the liquidation address. Please note, this functionality is not supported on Stellar.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-a-liquidation-address#response-state)

state

string

The state of the liquidation address. It could be "active" or "deactivated"

Liquidation Addresses

Get all Liquidation Addresses for a customer

Get all Liquidation Addresses for a customer

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/liquidation_addresses \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-all-liquidation-addresses-for-a-customer#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-all-liquidation-addresses-for-a-customer#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-all-liquidation-addresses-for-a-customer#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-all-liquidation-addresses-for-a-customer#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a liquidation address id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a liquidation address right AFTER the specified liquidation address id on the liquidation address timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that liquidation address older than the specified liquidation address id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-all-liquidation-addresses-for-a-customer#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a liquidation address id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a liquidation address right BEFORE the specified liquidation address id on the liquidation address timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that liquidation address newer than the specified liquidation address id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

#### Response

200

application/json

List of Liquidation Addresses (the returned list is empty if none found)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-all-liquidation-addresses-for-a-customer#response-count)

count

integer

required

total number of items in data

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/get-all-liquidation-addresses-for-a-customer#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Navigation

Get started

Get set up with Bridge

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/get-set-up-with-bridge#step-1-create-a-bridge-account)

Step 1: Create a Bridge account

**Are you an existing developer?** Head over to [dashboard.bridge.xyz](https://dashboard.bridge.xyz/)
 to login to your Bridge Dashboard. **Do you want to get started?** [Contact sales](https://www.bridge.xyz/requestfreedemo)
.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/get-set-up-with-bridge#step-2-create-your-api-keys)

Step 2: Create your API keys

Once logged in, click on the “API Keys” tab on the top menu bar and generate a new API key.

Safely store your API keys

Bridge will make your **API key available only once**, so make sure to **immediately copy and save the key safely and securely**. Your key is used to authenticate into our APIs and is highly sensitive. If it ever gets compromised, you can immediately revoke key access from our dashboard and generate a new key.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/get-set-up-with-bridge#step-3-follow-our-guides-and-start-moving-money)

Step 3: Follow our guides and start moving money.

[**Create your first customer**](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/create-your-first-customer)
 - This guide walks you through creating your first customer and getting them verified [**Create a one-time payment**](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/create-a-one-time-payment)
 - This guide walks you through moving funds onchain through a bank [**Setting up webhooks**](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/setting-up-webhooks)
 - This guide walks you through setting up and using Bridge webhooks to handle customer events in your application.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Platform overview](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/overview)
[Onboard your first customer](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/create-your-first-customer)

Update an External Account

cURL

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/external_accounts/{externalAccountID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "address": {
        "street_line_1": "<string>",
        "city": "<string>",
        "country": "<string>",
        "street_line_2": "<string>",
        "state": "<string>",
        "postal_code": "<string>"
      },
      "account": {
        "checking_or_savings": "checking",
        "routing_number": "<string>"
      }
    }
    '

200

*   ACH/Wire

US bank account using account and routing numbers for ACH or Wire transfers

id

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-customer-id)

customer\_id

string

required

The id of the Bridge customer that this External Account belongs to

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account-owner-name)

account\_owner\_name

string

required

Owner of the account Bank Account (e.g. "John Doe"). For ach or wire transfers, this field must be at least 3 characters, at most 35 characters, and follow either of the following regex patterns:

*   ach: `^(?!\s*$)[\x20-\x7E]*$`
*   wire: ``^[ \w!"#$%&'()+,\-./:;<=>?@\\_`~]*$``

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of creation of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

required

Time of last update of the External Account

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-active)

active

boolean

required

Whether or not this External Account is active

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account-type)

account\_type

enum<string>

required

Type of the bank account.

Available options:

`us`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

Currency associated with the bank account. Must be `usd` for US accounts.

Available options:

`usd`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account)

account

us · object

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-bank-name)

bank\_name

string

Bank name of the account (e.g. "Chase")

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account-owner-type)

account\_owner\_type

enum<string>

The type of the account ownership. Required when the `account_type` is `iban`. For `individual` ownership, `first_name` and `last_name` are required. For `business` ownership, `business_name` is required.

Available options:

`individual`,

`business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-first-name)

first\_name

string

First name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-last-name)

last\_name

string

Last name of the individual account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `individual`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-business-name)

business\_name

string

Business name of the business account holder. Required when the `account_owner_type` is `business`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-deactivation-reason)

deactivation\_reason

enum<string>

Reason for deactivation when this External Account is inactive

Available options:

`plaid_item_error`,

`deactivated_due_to_bounceback`,

`deleted_by_developer`,

`requested_by_developer`,

`invalid_account_number`,

`invalid_bank_validation`,

`rejected_by_bank_provider`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-deactivation-details)

deactivation\_details

string

Additional details about the deactivation when this External Account is inactive

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-beneficiary-address-valid)

beneficiary\_address\_valid

boolean

Whether the beneficiary address is valid. A valid beneficiary address is required for all US External Accounts

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-last-4)

last\_4

string

deprecated

Last 4 digits of the bank account number. This field is getting deprecated in favor of the `account.last_4` field

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/external-accounts/update-an-external-account#response-one-of-0-account-validation-one-of-0)

account\_validation

object

Present for Pix, SPEI/CLABE, and Bre-B accounts with a successful validation; contains validated owner and bank name.

Show child attributes

# Custodial wallets - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/overview#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Integrate custodial wallets

Custodial wallets

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Bridge offers fully managed, compliant custody for stablecoins with no third-party integrations required. Using Bridge wallets, you can:

*   Create wallets for your customers or your business.
*   Transfer stablecoins in and out using orchestration APIs.
*   Query balances and transfer history.
*   Tag and organize wallets as needed.

Before creating wallets, make sure you have onboarded your customer and finished any required KYC/KYB or endorsements.

Learn more at [wallets](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/wallets/overview)
.

YesNo

[BTC and ETH Support](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/move-money/btc-and-eth-support)
[Send fiat deposits to your wallet](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/onramp)

Create a funds withdrawal request

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)

[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Create a funds withdrawal request

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/card_accounts/{cardAccountID}/withdrawals \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "amount": "<string>",
      "destination": {
        "chain": "<string>",
        "address": "<string>",
        "memo": "<string>"
      },
      "type": "top_up_balance_withdrawal",
      "client_note": "<string>"
    }
    '

201

Example

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "card_account_id": "<string>",
      "customer_id": "<string>",
      "amount": "<string>",
      "currency": "usdc",
      "destination": {
        "chain": "<string>",
        "address": "<string>",
        "memo": "<string>",
        "tx_hash": "<string>"
      },
      "created_at": "<string>",
      "updated_at": "<string>",
      "type": "top_up_balance_withdrawal",
      "client_note": "<string>"
    }

Liquidation Addresses

Create a Liquidation Address

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Create a Liquidation Address

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/liquidation_addresses \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "currency": "usdb",
      "chain": "arbitrum",
      "external_account_id": "<string>",
      "prefunded_account_id": "<string>",
      "bridge_wallet_id": "<string>",
      "destination_wire_message": "<string>",
      "destination_sepa_reference": "<string>",
      "destination_ach_reference": "<string>",
      "destination_spei_reference": "<string>",
      "destination_reference": "<string>",
      "destination_payment_rail": "ach",
      "destination_currency": "brl",
      "destination_address": "<string>",
      "destination_blockchain_memo": "<string>",
      "return_address": "<string>",
      "custom_developer_fee_percent": "0.1"
    }
    '

201

SuccessfulLiquidationAddressCreateResponse

    {
      "id": "la_123",
      "chain": "ethereum",
      "customer_id": "cust_123",

      "currency": "usdc",
      "state": "active",
      "created_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",
      "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"

header
