Idempotency-Key

string

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Body

application/json

Liquidation Address object to be created

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

Available options:

`usdb`,

`usdc`,

`usdt`,

`dai`,

`pyusd`,

`eurc`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-chain)

chain

enum<string>

required

Available options:

`arbitrum`,

`avalanche_c_chain`,

`base`,

`celo`,

`ethereum`,

`optimism`,

`polygon`,

`solana`,

`stellar`,

`tempo`,

`tron`,

`evm`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-external-account-id)

external\_account\_id

string

External bank account to which Bridge will send the funds. The currency associated with the External Account must match the destination currency.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-prefunded-account-id)

prefunded\_account\_id

string

The developer's prefunded account id that Bridge will send the funds to.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-bridge-wallet-id)

bridge\_wallet\_id

string

The Bridge Wallet to which Bridge will send the funds. The chain associated with the Bridge Wallet must match the payment rail.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-wire-message)

destination\_wire\_message

string

A message to be sent with a wire transfer. It can have up to 140 characters. This message will be validated against 4 lines, each with a max length of 35 characters according to the Fedwire standard.

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-sepa-reference)

destination\_sepa\_reference

string

A reference message to be sent with a SEPA transaction. We recommend you set a unique value to help you and your customers track payments end to end. It must be from 6 to 140 characters. The allowed characters are `a-z`, `A-Z`, `0-9`, spaces, ampersand (`&`), hyphen (`-`), full stop (`.`), and solidus (`/`). If not populated, the default value is "Payment via Bridge {unique\_token}".

Required string length: `6 - 140`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-ach-reference)

destination\_ach\_reference

string

A reference message to be sent with an ACH transaction. It can be at most 10 characters, A-Z, a-z, 0-9, and spaces.

Required string length: `1 - 10`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-spei-reference)

destination\_spei\_reference

string

A payment reference message or remittance information to be included in a SPEI transaction. The allowed characters are alphanumeric `a-z`, `A-Z`, `0-9`, and space

Required string length: `1 - 40`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-reference)

destination\_reference

string

A payment reference message for newer payment rails (e.g. Pix).

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-payment-rail)

destination\_payment\_rail

enum<string>

The payment rail that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer. Will default to ACH if not specified.

Available options:

`ach`,

`wire`,

`ach_push`,

`ach_same_day`,

`arbitrum`,

`avalanche_c_chain`,

`base`,

`bre_b`,

`celo`,

`ethereum`,

`faster_payments`,

`fiat_deposit_return`,

`optimism`,

`pix`,

`polygon`,

`sepa`,

`solana`,

`spei`,

`stellar`,

`swift`,

`tempo`,

`tron`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-currency)

destination\_currency

enum<string>

The currency that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer. Will default to USD if not specified.

Available options:

`brl`,

`cop`,

`dai`,

`eur`,

`eurc`,

`gbp`,

`mxn`,

`pyusd`,

`usd`,

`usdb`,

`usdc`,

`usdt`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-address)

destination\_address

string

The crypto wallet address that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-blockchain-memo)

destination\_blockchain\_memo

string

The memo to include in the transaction, for blockchains that support memos only

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-return-address)

return\_address

string

The crypto wallet address that Bridge will use to return funds to the customer in case of a failed transaction. This address must be on the same chain specified for the liquidation address. Please note, this functionality is not supported on Stellar.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#body-custom-developer-fee-percent-one-of-0)

custom\_developer\_fee\_percent

string<number> | null

The developer fee percent that will be applied to this Liquidation Address or null to use the default fee. The value is a base 100 percentage, i.e. 10.2% is 10.2 in the API.

Example:

`"0.1"`

#### Response

201

application/json

Liquidation Address object created

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-currency)

currency

enum<string>

required

Available options:

`usdb`,

`usdc`,

`usdt`,

`dai`,

`pyusd`,

`eurc`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-chain)

chain

enum<string>

required

Available options:

`arbitrum`,

`avalanche_c_chain`,

`base`,

`celo`,

`ethereum`,

`optimism`,

`polygon`,

`solana`,

`stellar`,

`tempo`,

`tron`,

`evm`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-payment-rail)

destination\_payment\_rail

enum<string>

required

The payment rail that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer.

Available options:

`ach`,

`wire`,

`ach_push`,

`ach_same_day`,

`arbitrum`,

`avalanche_c_chain`,

`tron`

destination\_currency

enum<string>

required

The currency that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer.

Available options:

`brl`,

`cop`,

`dai`,

`eur`,

`eurc`,

`gbp`,

`mxn`,

`pyusd`,

`usd`,

`usdb`,

`usdc`,

`usdt`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-external-account-id)

external\_account\_id

string

External bank account to which Bridge will send the funds.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-prefunded-account-id)

prefunded\_account\_id

string

The developer's prefunded account to which Bridge will send the funds.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-bridge-wallet-id)

bridge\_wallet\_id

string

The Bridge Wallet to which Bridge will send the funds. The chain associated with the Bridge Wallet must match the payment rail.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-wire-message)

destination\_wire\_message

string

A message to be sent with a wire transfer.

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-sepa-reference)

destination\_sepa\_reference

string

A reference message to be sent with a SEPA transaction.

Required string length: `6 - 140`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-ach-reference)

destination\_ach\_reference

string

A reference message to be sent with an ACH transaction. It can be at most 10 characters, A-Z, a-z, 0-9, and spaces.

Required string length: `1 - 10`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-spei-reference)

destination\_spei\_reference

string

A payment reference message or remittance information to be included in a SPEI transaction. The allowed characters are alphanumeric `a-z`, `A-Z`, `0-9`, and space

Required string length: `1 - 40`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-reference)

destination\_reference

string

A payment reference message for newer payment rails (e.g. Pix).

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-address)

destination\_address

string

The crypto wallet address that Bridge will use to send funds to the customer.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-destination-blockchain-memo)

destination\_blockchain\_memo

string

The memo to include in the transaction, for blockchains that support memos only

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-return-address)

return\_address

string

The crypto wallet address that Bridge will use to return funds to the customer in case of a failed transaction. This address must be on the same chain specified for the liquidation address. Please note, this functionality is not supported on Stellar.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-custom-developer-fee-percent-one-of-0)

custom\_developer\_fee\_percent

string<number> | null

The developer fee percent that will be applied to this Liquidation Address or null to use the default fee. The value is a base 100 percentage, i.e. 10.2% is 10.2 in the API.

Example:

`"0.1"`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-address)

address

string

The blockchain address the customer will send funds to.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/create-a-liquidation-address#response-state)

state

string

The state of the liquidation address. It could be "active" or "deactivated"

# Supported blockchains and fiat rails - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/payment-routes#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

What we support

Supported blockchains and fiat rails

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

The following stablecoins and blockchains are supported across all Bridge APIs. Note that **USDB** is Bridge’s native stablecoin and **earns rewards automatically** when held. Interested in support for other assets or blockchains? **Contact us directly** to discuss integration.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/payment-routes#important)

Important

*   ⚠️ Deposits sent to **unsupported asset/blockchain pairs** or to **incorrect addresses** may be **irretrievable and permanently lost**.
*   Make sure that you are sending amounts above the **transaction minimum**, learn more about how minimums are enforced [here](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/fees-and-mins/mins)
    . Refer the below table for supported payment routes and transaction minimums.
*   **USDT and all Bridge issued stablecoins are not supported for users in the EEA** due to regulatory restrictions

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/payment-routes#supported-fiat-rails)

**Supported fiat rails**

*   ACH (USD)
*   Wire (USD)
*   SEPA (EUR)
*   SPEI (MXN)
*   Pix (BRL)
*   Faster Payments (GBP)
*   Bre-B & Bank Transfer (COP) - BETA
*   and more coming soon!

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/payment-routes#route-explorer)

**Route Explorer**

Below, you will find all the routes we support. You can use the filters to search for the routes you are interested in.

Liquidation Addresses

Update a Liquidation Address

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Update a Liquidation Address

cURL

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/liquidation_addresses/{liquidationAddressID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "external_account_id": "<string>",
      "custom_developer_fee_percent": "0.1",
      "destination_ach_reference": "<string>",
      "destination_wire_message": "<string>",
      "destination_sepa_reference": "<string>",
      "destination_spei_reference": "<string>",
      "return_address": "<string>"
    }
    '

200

SuccessfulLiquidationAddressUpdateResponse

    {
      "id": "la_123",
      "chain": "ethereum",
      "customer_id": "cust_123",
      "external_account_id": "ext_123",
      "address": "0x4d0280da2f2fDA5103914bCc5aad114743152A9c",
      "currency": "usdc",
      "destination_payment_rail": "wire",
      "destination_currency": "usd",
      "destination_wire_message": "a wire message",
      "state": "active",
      "created_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z",
      "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"
    }

PUT

/

customers

/

{customerID}

/

liquidation\_addresses

/

{liquidationAddressID}

Try it

Update a Liquidation Address

cURL

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/liquidation_addresses/{liquidationAddressID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "external_account_id": "<string>",
      "custom_developer_fee_percent": "0.1",
      "destination_ach_reference": "<string>",
      "destination_wire_message": "<string>",
      "destination_sepa_reference": "<string>",
      "destination_spei_reference": "<string>",
      "return_address": "<string>"
    }
    '

200

SuccessfulLiquidationAddressUpdateResponse

    {
      "id": "la_123",
      "chain": "ethereum",
      "customer_id": "cust_123",
      "external_account_id": "ext_123",
      "address": "0x4d0280da2f2fDA5103914bCc5aad114743152A9c",
      "currency": "usdc",
      "destination_payment_rail": "wire",
      "destination_currency": "usd",
      "destination_wire_message": "a wire message",
      "state": "active",

      "updated_at": "2023-11-22T21:31:30.515Z"
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#parameter-liquidation-address-id)

liquidationAddressID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Body

application/json

Liquidation Address details to be updated

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#body-external-account-id)

external\_account\_id

string

An optional identifier for the external account you wish to associate with this liquidation schedule.

Note: Only one liquidation address can be associated with an external account per (customer, chain, currency).

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#body-custom-developer-fee-percent-one-of-0)

custom\_developer\_fee\_percent

string<number> | null

The developer fee percent that will be applied to this Liquidation Address or null to use the default fee. The value is a base 100 percentage, i.e. 10.2% is 10.2 in the API.

Example:

`"0.1"`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-ach-reference)

destination\_ach\_reference

string

A reference message to be sent with an ACH transaction. It can be at most 10 characters, A-Z, a-z, 0-9, and spaces.

Required string length: `1 - 10`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-wire-message)

destination\_wire\_message

string

A message to be sent with a wire transfer. It can have up to 140 characters. This message will be validated against 4 lines, each with a max length of 35 characters according to the Fedwire standard.

Required string length: `1 - 256`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-sepa-reference)

destination\_sepa\_reference

string

A reference message to be sent with a SEPA transaction. We recommend you set a unique value to help you and your customers track payments end to end. It must be from 6 to 140 characters. The allowed characters are `a-z`, `A-Z`, `0-9`, spaces, ampersand (`&`), hyphen (`-`), full stop (`.`), and solidus (`/`). If not populated, the default value is "Payment via Bridge {unique\_token}".

Required string length: `6 - 140`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#body-destination-spei-reference)

destination\_spei\_reference

string

A payment reference message or remittance information to be included in a SPEI transaction. The allowed characters are alphanumeric `a-z`, `A-Z`, `0-9`, and space

Required string length: `1 - 40`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/liquidation-addresses/update-a-liquidation-address#body-return-address)

return\_address

string

The crypto wallet address that Bridge will use to return funds to the customer in case of a failed transaction. This address must be on the same chain specified for the liquidation address. Please note, this functionality is not supported on Stellar.

# Send fiat deposits to your wallet - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/onramp#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Integrate custodial wallets

Send fiat deposits to your wallet

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

This guide walks you through creating a crypto wallet for a customer, then linking it to a virtual account so fiat deposits (e.g. ACH, SEPA) are automatically converted and delivered to the wallet as stablecoins. ![](https://files.readme.io/d051ccd62a78c5556e3401e032c74ee265918ddd1aa35e45263bbb434b1253d3-image.png)

* * *

1

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/onramp#)

Step 1: Create a wallet
-----------------------

Create a new Bridge-managed crypto wallet for your customer. This wallet will hold funds (e.g. USDB) and can earn yield.

Request

    curl --request POST \
         --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/<customer_id>/wallets \
         --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
         --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique-Key>' \
         --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
         --data-raw '{
           "chain": "solana"
         }'
    

See all 8 lines

Response

    {
      "id": "wallet_abc123",
      "chain": "solana",
      "address": "4oG1sWkP8vcrnhbkzZc1m9RTT2VUjZHKx92qiVFK7FuZ",
      "created_at": "2025-07-15T18:00:00Z"
    }
    

See all 6 lines

Use the `bridge_wallet_id` (wallet\_abc123 above) when referencing the wallet in other Bridge APIs.

2

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/onramp#)

Step 2: Create a virtual account that onramps to the wallet
-----------------------------------------------------------

Now, link the wallet to a virtual account. Any fiat deposits into the account will be automatically converted to USDB and delivered to the wallet.

Request

    curl --request POST \
         --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/<customer_id>/virtual_accounts \
         --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
         --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique-Key>' \
         --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
         --data-raw '{
           "source": {
             "currency": "usd"
           },
           "destination": {
             "payment_rail": "solana",
             "currency": "usdb",
             "bridge_wallet_id": "wallet_abc123"
           }
         }'
    

See all 15 lines

Response

    {
      "id": "va_123",
      "status": "activated",
      "customer_id": "cust_alice",
      "source_deposit_instructions": {
        "currency": "usd",
        "bank_beneficiary_name": "Alice Customer",
        "bank_name": "Lead Bank",
        "bank_address": "1801 Main St., Kansas City, MO 64108",
        "bank_routing_number": "101019644",
        "bank_account_number": "123456789",
        "payment_rails": ["ach_push", "wire"],
      },
      "destination": {
        "bridge_wallet_id": "wallet_abc123",
        "currency": "usdb"
      }
    }
    

See all 18 lines

3

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/onramp#)

Step 3: Share the virtual account address
-----------------------------------------

Share the virtual account details (account and routing number) with your customer. When they send a fiat deposit, Bridge will:

*   Match the payment
*   Convert it to stablecoin (e.g. USDB)
*   Deliver it to the linked wallet

4

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/onramp#)

Step 4: Check wallet balance
----------------------------

Use this API to check wallet balances and confirm the funds have landed.

Request

    curl --request GET  
         --url <https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/customerId/wallets/walletId>  
         --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>'  
         --header 'accept: application/json'
    

See all 4 lines

Response

    {  
      "id": "uuid",  
      "chain": "solana",  
      "address": "the-blockchain-address",  
      "created_at": "2024-09-01T02:03:04.567Z",  
      "updated_at": "2024-09-01T02:03:04.567Z",  
      "balances": [  \
        {\
          "balance": "123.456789",\
          "currency": "usdb",  \
          "chain": "solana",\
          "contract_address": "ENL66PGy8d8j5KNqLtCcg4uidDUac5ibt45wbjH9REzB",  \
        }  \
      ]  
    }
    

See all 15 lines

YesNo

[Send wallet funds to a crypto address](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/crypto-to-crypto)

required

required

has\_ownership

boolean

True if this person has at least 25% ownership of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/delete-a-single-associated-person#response-has-control)

has\_control

boolean

True if this is the control person of the company, having significant responsibility to control, manage or influence the activities of the business entity.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/delete-a-single-associated-person#response-is-signer)

is\_signer

boolean

True if this person is able to authorize transactions on behalf of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/delete-a-single-associated-person#response-title)

title

string

The title of this associated person at the company, e.g. CEO, CFO, etc.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/delete-a-single-associated-person#response-attested-ownership-structure-at)

attested\_ownership\_structure\_at

string

When this individual attested to the correctness of the ownership structure provided to Bridge. If provided by at least one control person, ownership documents for the business are not required.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/delete-a-single-associated-person#response-relationship-established-at)

relationship\_established\_at

string

When the associated person relationship was established in format yyyy-mm-dd.

# Platform overview - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/overview#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Get started

Platform overview

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Bridge APIs are modular building blocks that let you create fast, flexible, and compliant payment experiences. Whether you’re collecting fiat, moving stablecoins, or issuing cards, our APIs are designed to support your unique use case — across fiat and crypto. This guide outlines the **core product categories**, what each product does, and **when you should use them**.

* * *

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/overview#-orchestration-move-money)

🔁 Orchestration: Move money
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bridge orchestration APIs power your fiat and crypto flows. Go from fiat to crypto (onramps), crypto to fiat (offramps), and crypto to crypto.

| Product | Description | Use when you need to… |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Virtual Accounts** | **Unique fiat deposit addresses** (ACH, Wire, SEPA, SPEI) issued to your customers. | Collect fiat bank transfers - especially for recurring deposits. |
| **Transfers** | **One-time fiat or stablecoin transfers**. Supports onramps, offramps, and crypto-to-crypto flows. | When you need to send or receive money programmatically - either fiat or crypto. |
| **Static Template Transfers** | **Reusable transfer instructions** for **recurring**, template-based transfers. AKA payment routes in dashboard | Let customers make recurring payments. |
| **Liquidation Addresses** | **On-chain addresses** that auto-forward to a crypto or fiat destination. | Accept crypto at fixed addresses and automatically route or convert funds. |
| **Prefunded Accounts** | Load fiat into Bridge-managed balances for instant offramps. | **Guarantee fast withdrawals** without waiting for inbound deposits to settle. |

* * *

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/overview#-wallets-custody-crypto)

👜 Wallets: Custody crypto
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bridge offers secure custodial wallets that allow you to hold and transfer stablecoins — with full compliance built-in. You can provision wallets for your customers or even for yourself to help with treasury management.

| **Product** | **Description** | **Use When You Need To…** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Bridge Wallets** | Custodial wallets for managing crypto on behalf of users or your business. | Custody crypto and power stablecoin transfers. |

* * *

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/overview#-cards-spend-stablecoins-anywhere)

💳 Cards: Spend stablecoins anywhere
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Let users spend their stablecoin balances globally using virtual Visa cards.

| **Product** | **Description** | **Use When You Need To…** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Cards** | Issue virtual cards linked to Bridge or external wallets. | When you want to enable customers to spend stablecoin balances anywhere Visa is accepted globally. |

* * *

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/overview#-issuance-create-or-use-stablecoins)

🪙 Issuance: Create or use stablecoins
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use Bridge’s stablecoin (USDB) or launch your own branded version.

| **Product** | **Description** | **Use When You Need To…** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **USDB / Custom Stablecoins** | Mint USDB or branded stablecoins that earn yield on held balances. | Offer branded stablecoins, or earn yield on reserve balances. |

* * *

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/overview#-customers-onboarding-&-compliance)

👤 Customers: Onboarding & compliance
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bridge provides built-in tools to onboard and manage your users with full KYC/KYB compliance.

| **Product** | **Description** | **Use When You Need To…** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Customer Onboarding** | Verify identity and onboard customers across financial rails and products. | Onboard users to new payment products and need to satisfy compliance requirements. |

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Welcome](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Get set up with Bridge](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/get-set-up-with-bridge)

⌘I

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-static-templates-for-a-customer#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-static-templates-for-a-customer#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a transfer id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a transfer right AFTER the specified transfer id on the transfer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that transfers older than the specified transfer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-static-templates-for-a-customer#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a transfer id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a transfer right BEFORE the specified transfer id on the transfer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that transfers newer than the specified transfer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

#### Response

200

application/json

List of static templates (the returned list is empty if none found)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-static-templates-for-a-customer#response-count)

count

integer

required

The number of static templates returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-static-templates-for-a-customer#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

This is a customer id. This also implies that customers older than the specified customer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

ending\_before

string

If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a customer right BEFORE the specified customer id on the customer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that customers newer than the specified customer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

# Set up a sandbox environment - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/setting-up-sandbox#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Get started

Set up a sandbox environment

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Bridge has a sandbox environment for you to quickly begin testing your integration without having to move real money. To access this sandbox, you must first reach out to [support@bridge.xyz](mailto:support@bridge.xyz)
 to get onboarded with a Developer account within Bridge. Afterwards, you’ll be able to generate sandbox API keys

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/setting-up-sandbox#step-1-generate-a-sandbox-key)

Step 1: Generate a Sandbox Key
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Note that only dashboard admins have access to both sandbox and prod API keys.**  
Please ask your dashboard admin for access if you don’t have it

*   Go to [https://dashboard.bridge.xyz/](https://dashboard.bridge.xyz/)
     and log in with your email.
*   Then, ensure the “Sandbox” toggle is turned on (blue).
*   Then, hit the button to generate a sandbox key.
*   Sandbox keys should be prefixed with `sk-test`.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/setting-up-sandbox#step-2-hit-an-api)

Step 2: Hit an API
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bridge’s sandbox is currently functional with the customer creation and KYC process. For example, here is how you can create a Bridge customer.

**Note that the sandbox base url is** [https://api.sandbox.bridge.xyz](https://api.sandbox.bridge.xyz/)

    curl --location --request POST 'https://api.sandbox.bridge.xyz/v0/customers' \
    --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
    --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
    --header 'Idempotency-Key: <generate a uuid>' \
    --data-raw '{
      "first_name": "John",
      "last_name": "Doe",
      "email": "johndoe@johndoe.com",
      "address": {
        "street_line_1": "123 Washington St",
        "street_line_2": "Apt 2F",
        "city": "San Francisco",
        "state": "CA",
        "postal_code": "10001",
        "country": "USA"
      },
      "birth_date": "1989-09-09",
      "tax_identification_number": "111-11-1111",
      "phone": "+15555555555",
      "signed_agreement_id": "<generate a uuid>",
      "type": "individual"
    }'
    

See all 22 lines

We recommend the following steps to get a sense of how to use Bridge:

*   Create a customer
*   Fetch that customer
*   Examine simulated KYC
*   Creating fake liquidation addresses, transfers and fiat deposit instructions (Note: there is no real money movement in Sandbox)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/setting-up-sandbox#differences-with-production)

Differences with Production
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sandbox differs from production in a few key areas. We highly recommend using the Sandbox only to test API request/response schemas and Production itself for any other kind of testing. **Onboarding/KYC**

*   Customers must be created via the API; they cannot be created using kyc links.
*   Customers are automatically approved (no KYC/KYB flow)
*   Sandbox is subject to arbitrary rate limits; we may drop your requests anytime.
*   The signed agreement ID in production cannot be arbitrary
*   While in production you can have multiple users under the same Developer Account, in Sandbox each of those users will be scoped under their own unique Developer Account. In particular, changes made by one user in the sandbox won’t be visible to other users **even if those users share a developer account in production**.

**Payments**

*   There is no real money movement in Sandbox.
*   Plaid does not work in Sandbox.
*   There is no testnet support in Sandbox.
*   Virtual Accounts, Static Memos, Liquidation Addresses, and Transfers are created with dummy data.
*   There are no payments-related webhooks fired in sandbox.

Wallets and Stablecoin Issuance are only supported in Production If you have suggests for how to improve our sandbox experience, please reach out to us at [support@bridge.xyz](mailto:support@bridge.xyz)
, thanks!

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Configure webhooks](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/setting-up-webhooks)
[Supported blockchains and fiat rails](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/what-we-support/payment-routes)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Customers

Get a single customer object

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Get a single customer object

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulCustomerResponse

    {
      "id": "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
      "first_name": "John",
      "last_name": "Doe",
      "email": "johndoe@example.com",
      "status": "active",
      "type": "individual",
      "persona_inquiry_type": "gov_id_db",

      "updated_at": "2025-11-19T21:16:02.894Z",
      "rejection_reasons": [],
      "has_accepted_terms_of_service": true,
      "endorsements": [\
        {\
          "name": "base",\
          "status": "approved",\
          "requirements": {\
            "complete": [\
              "terms_of_service_v1",\
              "first_name",\

Get a single customer object

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

SuccessfulCustomerResponse

    {
      "id": "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Response

200

application/json

Successful customer object response

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-id)

id

string

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-first-name)

first\_name

string

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-last-name)

last\_name

string

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-email)

email

string

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-status)

status

enum<string>

`offboarded`: represents a customer's account that was internally reviewed and closed due to suspicious activity. `paused`: represents a customer's account that is currently under review because of activity on the platform.

Available options:

`active`,

`awaiting_questionnaire`,

`awaiting_ubo`,

`incomplete`,

`not_started`,

`offboarded`,

`paused`,

`rejected`,

`under_review`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-capabilities)

capabilities

object

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-future-requirements-due)

future\_requirements\_due

enum<string>\[\]

Information about requirements that may be needed in the future for the customer (eg. enhanced KYC checks for high volume transactions etc.). Please consult our KYC guide on how to resolve each requirement.

Available options:

`id_verification`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-requirements-due)

requirements\_due

enum<string>\[\]

KYC requirements still needed to be completed. Please consult our KYC guide on how to resolve each requirement.

Available options:

`external_account`,

`id_verification`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-created-at)

created\_at

string<date-time>

Time of creation of the customer

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

Time of last update of the customer

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-rejection-reasons)

rejection\_reasons

object\[\]

Reasons why a customer KYC was rejected

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-has-accepted-terms-of-service)

has\_accepted\_terms\_of\_service

boolean

Whether the customer has accepted the terms of service.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-a-single-customer-object#response-endorsements)

endorsements

object\[\]

A summary of whether the customer has received approvals to complete onboarding or use certain products/services offered by Bridge.

Show child attributes

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# Retrieve a hosted KYC Link for an existing customer - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/retrieve-a-hosted-kyc-link-for-an-existing-customer#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Navigation

Customers

Retrieve a hosted KYC Link for an existing customer

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Retrieve a hosted KYC Link for an existing customer

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/kyc_link \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

KycLink

    {
      "url": "https://bridge.withpersona.com/verify?inquiry-template-id=itmpl_NtIXpb9AbEYCPxGo5iRbc9d2&reference-id=75d2f259-6810-4cde-a9b9-83eca42b0ebf"
    }

GET

/

customers

/

{customerID}

/

kyc\_link

Try it

Retrieve a hosted KYC Link for an existing customer

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/kyc_link \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

KycLink

    {
      "url": "https://bridge.withpersona.com/verify?inquiry-template-id=itmpl_NtIXpb9AbEYCPxGo5iRbc9d2&reference-id=75d2f259-6810-4cde-a9b9-83eca42b0ebf"
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/retrieve-a-hosted-kyc-link-for-an-existing-customer#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/retrieve-a-hosted-kyc-link-for-an-existing-customer#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/retrieve-a-hosted-kyc-link-for-an-existing-customer#parameter-endorsement)

endorsement

enum<string>

An endorsement is the approval required for a customer to use a particular product or service offered by Bridge

Available options:

`sepa`,

`spei`,

`cards`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/retrieve-a-hosted-kyc-link-for-an-existing-customer#parameter-redirect-uri)

redirect\_uri

string

An optional url encoded link that users will be redirected to after completing the hosted KYC flow.

Example:

`"http%3A%2F%2Fexample.com%2Fredirect"`

#### Response

200

application/json

A Hosted URL for KYC

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/retrieve-a-hosted-kyc-link-for-an-existing-customer#response-url)

url

string

required

A hosted KYC link

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Retrieve a hosted URL for ToS acceptance for an existing customer](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/retrieve-a-hosted-url-for-tos-acceptance-for-an-existing-customer)
[Get all transfers](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# Delete a single customer object - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/delete-a-single-customer-object#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Customers

Delete a single customer object

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Delete a single customer object

cURL

    curl --request DELETE \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

DeletedCustomerResponse

    {
      "id": "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",

# Send wallet funds to a crypto address - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/crypto-to-crypto#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Integrate custodial wallets

Send wallet funds to a crypto address

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Bridge wallets are secure, custodial crypto wallets that let you send and receive stablecoins with ease. Once you’ve provisioned a wallet for your customer or company, you can send and receive funds using orchestration API.

You must use Bridge’s orchestration APIs to move funds. **Do not attempt to send directly** from the wallet address.

![](https://files.readme.io/bcd6a3bfe25913355630174c61719239120611cd39ded4ffb188eaecd2a7bb07-image.png)

* * *

1

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/crypto-to-crypto#)

Step 1: Create a Bridge wallet
------------------------------

Request

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/<customer_id>/wallets \
      --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique Key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data-raw '{
        "chain": "solana"
      }'
    

See all 8 lines

Response

    {
      "id": "wallet_123",
      "chain": "solana",
      "address": "the-blockchain-address",
      "created_at": "2024-09-01T02:03:04.567Z",
      "updated_at": "2024-09-01T02:03:04.567Z"
    }
    

See all 7 lines

Note the `id` returned — this is your `bridge_wallet_id`.

2

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/crypto-to-crypto#)

Step 2: Transfer funds from wallet to crypto address
----------------------------------------------------

Use the [Transfers](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/transfers/create-a-transfer)
 API with `bridge_wallet` as the source.

Request

    curl --location --request POST 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/transfers' \
      --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique Key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data-raw '{
        "amount": "10.0",
        "on_behalf_of": "<customer_id>",
        "developer_fee": "0.0",
        "source": {
          "payment_rail": "bridge_wallet",
          "currency": "usdb",
          "bridge_wallet_id": "wallet_123"
        },
        "destination": {
          "payment_rail": "ethereum",
          "currency": "usdc",
          "to_address": "0xdeadbeef..."
        }
      }'
    

See all 19 lines

Response

    {
      "id": "transfer_abc",
      "amount": "10.0",
    	...
      "source": {
         "payment_rail": "bridge_wallet",
         "currency": "usdb",
         "bridge_wallet_id": "wallet_123"
       },
      "destination": {
        "payment_rail": "ethereum",
        "currency": "usdc",
        "to_address": "0xdeadbeef"
      },
    }
    

See all 15 lines

This will initiate a crypto transfer from your Bridge wallet to the specified blockchain address.

3

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/crypto-to-crypto#)

Step 3: Monitor transfer status (optional)
------------------------------------------

Use the Transfer ID returned in the response to monitor progress via the [Get a transfer](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/transfers/get-a-transfer)
 endpoint or by listening to webhooks — learn more at [Setting up webhooks](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/setting-up-webhooks)
.

Request

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/transfers/<transfer_id> \
      --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>'
    

See all 4 lines

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Send fiat deposits to your wallet](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/onramp)
[Send wallet funds to a fiat external account](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/wallets/offramp)

⌘I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos-for-customer#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos-for-customer#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos-for-customer#parameter-status)

status

enum<string>

Limit results to those with the given activation status The activation status of the Virtual Account

Available options:

`activated`,

`deactivated`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos-for-customer#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos-for-customer#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a static memo id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a static memo right AFTER the specified static memo id on the static memo timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that static memo older than the specified static memo id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos-for-customer#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a static memo id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a static memo right BEFORE the specified static memo id on the static memo timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that static memo newer than the specified static memo id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

#### Response

200 - application/json

List of Static Memos

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos-for-customer#response-count)

count

integer

required

total number of items in data

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos-for-customer#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

# Spend wallet balances using a card - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Provision and make card payments

Spend wallet balances using a card

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

You can issue a virtual or physical card that spends directly from a Bridge-managed wallet or external crypto wallet. Here’s how to set that up. ![](https://files.readme.io/abd125101ad0ef13134d7af37f6937eaaaa254bb7824de1552694da371805f0c-image.png)

* * *

1

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#)

Step 1: Prepare a Bridge wallet
-------------------------------

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#create-a-wallet)

Create a wallet

First, create a Bridge wallet (optional if you’re using an external wallet). Use the wallet’s `address` when issuing a card.

Request

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/<customer_id>/wallets \
      --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '{
        "chain": "solana"
      }'
    

See all 8 lines

Response

    {
      "id": "wallet_abc123",
      "address": "4oG1sWkP8vcrnhbkzZc1m9RTT2VUjZHKx92qiVFK7FuZ",
      "chain": "solana"
    }
    

See all 5 lines

Keep note of the wallet ID and address as you will need this in the next step.

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#fund-the-wallet)

Fund the wallet

The below example uses Bridge’s transfer API to fund the wallet. There are a variety of methods to fund the wallet using Bridge’s orchestration APIs (virtual accounts, transfers, or liquidation addresses). Learn more at [Bridge Wallets](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/wallets/overview)
.

    curl --location --request POST 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/transfers' \
    --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
    --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique Idempotency Key>' \
    --data-raw '{
      "on_behalf_of": "cust_alice",
      "source": {
        "payment_rail": "ach_push",
        "currency": "usd",
      },
      "destination": {
         "payment_rail": "solana",
         "currency": "usdb",
         "bridge_wallet_id": "wallet_abc123"
         }
         "features": {
           "flexible_amount": true // allows for any deposit amount
     		 }
    }'
    

See all 18 lines

2

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#)

Step 2: Provision a card
------------------------

Now create a card account tied to a Bridge wallet.

    curl --request POST \
         --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/customerID/card_accounts \
         --header 'accept: application/json' \
         --header 'content-type: application/json' \
         --data '{
      "currency": "usdb",
      "chain": "solana",
      "crypto_account": {
        "type": "bridge_wallet",
        "address": "4oG1sWkP8vcrnhbkzZc1m9RTT2VUjZHKx92qiVFK7FuZ"
      }
    }'
    

See all 12 lines

### 

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#retrieve-card-details)

Retrieve card details

Access card metadata, expiration, and access a secure image of the card.

Request

    curl -X GET 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/<customerID>/card_accounts/<cardAccountID>' \
    --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>'
    

See all 2 lines

Response

    {
      "id": "XXX-YYY",
      "status": "active",
      "card_image_url": "https://...",
      "card_details": {
        "last_4": "1264",
        "expiry": "10/24",
        "bin": "44325280"
      }
    }
    

See all 10 lines

You can now share these card details with your customer to **start spending!**

3

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#)

Step 3: Make a transaction
--------------------------

Now that you have the details for your card, you can use it to make transactions! Use your Bridge issued card like any normal card in e-commerce checkout flows.

4

[](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#)

Step 4: Monitor transactions
----------------------------

Subscribe to the `card_transaction.created` webhook to see newly created transactions.

    {
      "event_type": "card_transaction.created",
      "event_object": {
        "status": "approved",
        "amount": "-10.25",
        "merchant_name": "ROCKET RIDES",
        "authorized_at": "2025-02-04T05:19:25.000Z"
      }
    }
    

Subscribe to the `card_transaction.updated.status_transitioned` webhook to see settled transactions.

    {
      "event_type": "card_transaction.updated.status_transitioned",
      "event_object": {
        "status": "settled",
        "settled_amount": "-10.25",
        "posted_at": "2025-02-06T03:01:30.000Z"
      },
      "event_object_changes": {
        "status": ["approved", "settled"],
        "settled_amount": [null, "-10.25"],
        "posted_at": [null, "2025-02-06T03:01:30.000Z"]
      }
    }
    

Or you can fetch transactions via the [Retrieve card transactions](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/retrieve-card-transactions)
 API.

* * *

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#money-movement-overview)

Money Movement Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://files.readme.io/6929a243e3e872e7d1dcfd126c26611127127713f65bd0f0c92e4fd921ec4642-image.png)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/cards/spend#resources)

Resources
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check out the [Cards](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/cards/overview/overview)
 section for more in depth details!

# Create a new associated person for a business customer - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Customers

Create a new associated person for a business customer

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Create a new associated person for a business customer

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/associated_persons \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "first_name": "<string>",
      "last_name": "<string>",
      "email": "<string>",
      "residential_address": {
        "street_line_1": "<string>",
        "city": "<string>",
        "country": "<string>",
        "street_line_2": "<string>",
        "subdivision": "<string>",
        "postal_code": "<string>"
      },
      "birth_date": "<string>",
      "has_ownership": true,
      "has_control": true,
      "is_signer": true,
      "identifying_information": [\
        {\
          "type": "drivers_license",\
          "issuing_country": "<string>",\
          "number": "<string>",\
          "description": "<string>",\
          "expiration": "<string>",\
          "image_front": "<string>",\
          "image_back": "<string>"\
        }\
      ],
      "middle_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_first_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_middle_name": "<string>",
      "transliterated_last_name": "<string>",
      "phone": "<string>",
      "is_director": true,
      "title": "<string>",
      "ownership_percentage": 123,
      "attested_ownership_structure_at": "<string>",

string

The persons primary email address

residential\_address

object

required

The residential address of the associated person. This must be a physical address and cannot be a PO Box.

Show child attributes

birth\_date

string

required

Date of birth in format yyyy-mm-dd. Must be at least 18 years old.

Required string length: `10`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#body-has-ownership)

has\_ownership

boolean

required

True if this person has at least 25% ownership of the business.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#body-has-control)

has\_control

boolean

required

True if this is the control person of the company, having significant responsibility to control, manage or influence the activities of the business entity. At least one control person must be specified.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#body-is-signer)

is\_signer

boolean

required

True if this person is able to authorize transactions on behalf of the business. At least one signer must be specified.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#body-identifying-information)

identifying\_information

The middle name of the associated person

string

object

boolean

title

string

The title of this associated person at the company, e.g. CEO, CFO, etc. Required if has\_control is true.

Required string length: `1 - 1024`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#body-ownership-percentage)

integer

Ultimate ownership percentage of the business.

attested\_ownership\_structure\_at

string

The date or timestamp when this individual attested to the correctness of the ownership structure provided to Bridge. If provided by at least one control person, ownership documents for the business are not required.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#body-relationship-established-at)

relationship\_established\_at

string

The date or timestamp when the associated person relationship was established in format yyyy-mm-dd.

verified\_govid\_at

string

The date or timestamp for when individual's government ID was successfully verified.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#body-verified-selfie-at)

verified\_selfie\_at

string

The date or timestamp for when individual's selfie was successfully verified.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/create-a-new-associated-person-for-a-business-customer#body-completed-customer-safety-check-at)

completed\_customer\_safety\_check\_at

string

The date or timestamp for when individual successfully passed customer safety check.

Create a Static Memo

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/static_memos \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <idempotency-key>' \
      --data '
    {
      "source": {
        "currency": "usd",
        "payment_rail": "wire"
      },
      "destination": {
        "currency": "usdc",
        "payment_rail": "polygon",
        "address": "0xdeadbeef"
      },
      "developer_fee_percent": "0.1"
    }
    '

200

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "developer_fee_percent": "0.1",
      "source_deposit_instructions": {
        "currency": "usd",
        "payment_rails": [\
          "ach_push",\
          "wire"\
        ],
        "deposit_message": "EXAMPLE_MEMO_MESSAGE",
        "bank_name": "Lead Bank",
        "bank_address": "1801 Main St., Kansas City, MO 64108",
        "bank_beneficiary_name": "Bridge Ventures Inc",
        "bank_beneficiary_address": "21750 Hardy Oak Blvd, Ste 104 PMB 77950, San Antonio, Texas, 78258-4946",
        "bank_account_number": "123456789",
        "bank_routing_number": "87654321"
      },
      "destination": {
        "currency": "usdc",
        "payment_rail": "polygon",
        "address": "0xdeadbeef"
      },
      "created_at": "2023-11-07T05:31:56Z"

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-static-memo-id)

staticMemoID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-deposit-id)

deposit\_id

string

The deposit id associated with the events. Cannot be passed if deposit\_ids is also passed

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-deposit-ids)

deposit\_ids

string\[\]

The deposit ids associated with the events. Pass a list of deposit ids like "deposit\_ids\[\]=id1&deposit\_ids\[\]=id2". Cannot be passed if deposit\_id is also passed

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-tx-hash)

tx\_hash

string

The hash of the transaction

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is an event id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with an event right AFTER the specified event id on the event timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that events older than the specified event id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is an event id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with an event right BEFORE the specified event id on the event timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that events newer than the specified event id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#parameter-event-type)

event\_type

enum<string>

Filter history by event type

Available options:

`funds_received`,

`payment_submitted`,

`payment_processed`,

`in_review`,

`refund`,

`refund_in_flight`,

`refund_failed`,

`microdeposit`,

`account_update`,

`deactivation`,

`activation`

#### Response

200 - application/json

List of Static Memo events

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#response-count)

count

integer

required

The number of events returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/static-memo-activity#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos#parameter-status)

status

enum<string>

Limit results to those with the given activation status The activation status of the Virtual Account

Available options:

`activated`,

`deactivated`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a static memo id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a static memo right AFTER the specified static memo id on the static memo timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that static memo older than the specified static memo id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/list-static-memos#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a static memo id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a static memo right BEFORE the specified static memo id on the static memo timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that static memo newer than the specified static memo id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

List of Static Memos

required

total number of items in data

data

string

header

required

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/transfers/get-all-static-templates#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/transfers/get-all-static-templates#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a transfer id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a transfer right AFTER the specified transfer id on the transfer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that transfers older than the specified transfer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/transfers/get-all-static-templates#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a transfer id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a transfer right BEFORE the specified transfer id on the transfer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that transfers newer than the specified transfer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

#### Response

200

application/json

List of static templates (the returned list is empty if none found). Static templates are transfers that are used as templates for other transfers and can be created using the static\_templates feature flag.

count

integer

required

# Update a Static Memo - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/static-memos/update-a-static-memo#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Static Memos

Update a Static Memo

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Update a Static Memo

cURL

    curl --request PUT \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/static_memos/{staticMemoID} \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "destination": {
        "currency": "usdc",
        "payment_rail": "polygon",
        "address": "0xdeadbeef"
      },
      "developer_fee_percent": "0.1"
    }
    '

200

    {
      "id": "<string>",

Generate a card statement using Stripe IDs

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/cardholders/{cardholderID}/cards/{cardID}/statements/{period}.pdf \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

Example

    "<string>"

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/generate-a-card-statement-using-stripe-ids#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/generate-a-card-statement-using-stripe-ids#parameter-cardholder-id)

cardholderID

string

required

The Stripe cardholder ID (e.g. `ich_...`)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/generate-a-card-statement-using-stripe-ids#parameter-card-id)

cardID

string

required

period

string

required

A string in the `YYYYMM` format representing a card statement period

#### Response

200

application/pdf

The HTTP response that includes a PDF file as an attachment, with the `Content-Type` set to `application/pdf` and the `Content-Disposition` header configured to indicate it is a statement PDF attachment

The response is of type `file`.
