Try it

Get a summary of your card program

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/developer/cards/summary \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

Example

    {
      "period": "year",
      "period_starting": "2025-01-01",
      "cards_provisioned_count": 1123,
      "card_transactions_count": 31415,
      "provisioned_cards_by_country": {
        "USA": 123,
        "MEX": 45
      },
      "transaction_volume": "-100.0",
      "transacting_card_accounts_count": 2047,
      "card_transactions_count_by_country": {
        "USA": 74,
        "MEX": 55
      },
      "transaction_volume_by_country": {
        "USA": "7.04",
        "MEX": "5.0"
      },
      "transacting_cards_by_country": {
        "USA": 123,
        "MEX": 45
      }
    }

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#parameter-period)

period

enum<string>

required

The type of period to summarize the card program by. If `lifetime` is specified, the `period_key` is not required.

Available options:

`year`,

`month`,

`week`,

`day`,

`lifetime`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#parameter-period-key)

period\_key

string

A string to indicate the period to retrieve the card program summary for.

*   For `year`, the period key should be in the `YYYY` format
*   For `month`, the period key should be in the `YYYYMM` format
*   For `week`, the period key should be in the `YYYYMMDD` format indicating the beginning day of the week.
*   For `day`, the period key should be in the `YYYYMMDD` format
*   For `lifetime`, the period key is not required Note that if a specific period is specified, this endpoint currently only supports fetching for periods with complete data (e.g. only up to the previous year, month, week, or day).

#### Response

200

application/json

The summary of a card program

The summary of a card program for a given period

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-period)

period

enum<string>

The period type of the card program summary

Available options:

`year`,

`month`,

`week`,

`day`,

`lifetime`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-period-starting)

period\_starting

string

The starting date of the period, in ISO8601 format

Example:

`"2025-01-01"`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-cards-provisioned-count)

cards\_provisioned\_count

integer

The number of cards provisioned during the period

Example:

`1123`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-card-transactions-count)

card\_transactions\_count

integer

The number of card transactions during the period, excluding refunds.

Example:

`31415`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-provisioned-cards-by-country)

provisioned\_cards\_by\_country

object

The number of cards provisioned during the period, by issuing country. The key is the ISO-3166-1 alpha-3 country code, and the value is the number of cards provisioned for that issuing country.

Example:

    { "USA": 123, "MEX": 45 }

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-transaction-volume)

transaction\_volume

string

The total transaction volume during the period, in USD

Example:

`"-100.0"`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-transacting-card-accounts-count)

transacting\_card\_accounts\_count

integer

The number of card accounts that transacted during the period

Example:

`2047`

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-card-transactions-count-by-country)

card\_transactions\_count\_by\_country

object

The number of card transactions during the period, by merchant country. The key is the ISO-3166-1 alpha-3 country code, and the value is the number of card transactions for that merchant country.

Example:

    { "USA": 74, "MEX": 55 }

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-transaction-volume-by-country)

transaction\_volume\_by\_country

object

The transaction volume during the period, by merchant country. The key is the ISO-3166-1 alpha-3 country code, and the value is the transaction volume for that merchant country.

Example:

    { "USA": "7.04", "MEX": "5.0" }

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/cards/get-a-summary-of-your-card-program#response-transacting-cards-by-country)

transacting\_cards\_by\_country

object

The number of cards that transacted during the period, by issuing country. The key is the ISO-3166-1 alpha-3 country code, and the value is the number of cards transacted for that issuing country.

Example:

    { "USA": 123, "MEX": 45 }

Get all transfers

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{customerID}/transfers \
      --header 'Api-Key: <api-key>'

200

TransfersFound

      "count": 2,

          "$ref": "#/components/examples/AchOfframpTransferResponse/value"\

      ]

#### Authorizations

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#authorization-api-key)

Api-Key

string

header

required

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#parameter-customer-id)

customerID

string

required

A UUID that uniquely identifies a resource

Required string length: `1 - 42`

Pattern: `[a-z0-9]*`

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

The number of items to return (default of 10, max of 100)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#parameter-starting-after)

starting\_after

string

This is a transfer id. If this is specified, the next page that starts with a transfer right AFTER the specified transfer id on the transfer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that transfers older than the specified transfer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if ending\_before is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#parameter-ending-before)

ending\_before

string

This is a transfer id. If this is specified, the previous page that ends with a transfer right BEFORE the specified transfer id on the transfer timeline, which is always ordered from the newest to the oldest by creation time, will be returned. This also implies that transfers newer than the specified transfer id will be returned (shouldn't be set if starting\_after is set)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#parameter-tx-hash)

tx\_hash

string

The hash of the transaction

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#parameter-updated-after-ms)

updated\_after\_ms

integer

This is a unix timestamp in milliseconds. If this is specified, objects updated AFTER the specified timestamp will be returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#parameter-updated-before-ms)

updated\_before\_ms

integer

This is a unix timestamp in milliseconds. If this is specified, objects updated BEFORE the specified timestamp will be returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#parameter-state)

state

enum<string>

Filter transfers by their external state. See [Transfer States](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/transfers/transfer-states)
 for more details.

Available options:

`awaiting_funds`,

`funds_received`,

`payment_submitted`,

`payment_processed`,

`in_review`,

`kyc_required`,

`kyc_in_review`,

`developer_kyb_required`,

`canceled`,

`error`,

`returned`,

`refund_in_flight`,

`refund_failed`,

`refunded`,

`undeliverable`

#### Response

200

application/json

List of transfers (the returned list is empty if none found)

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#response-count)

count

integer

required

The number of transfers returned

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/customers/get-all-transfers#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

# Payroll - Bridge

[Skip to main content](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/common-use-cases/payroll#content-area)

[Bridge home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/logo/bridge_logo.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=3da6f2e8f14f2b938d7a051e797ffc2d)](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)

⌘KAsk AI

Navigation

Common use cases

Payroll

[Home](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/)
[Get Started](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/overview)
[Developer Platform](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/platform/orchestration/overview)
[API reference](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/introduction/introduction)
[Changelog](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/changelog/changelog)

Enable employers to pay employees and contractors globally by creating a wallet and virtual account for the employer and a wallet for each employee. Fiat deposits into the virtual account are converted to stablecoins and held in the employer’s wallet. Use the Transfers API to pay out funds from the employer to the employee. ![Payroll.png](https://mintcdn.com/bridge-727305d3/cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k/images/Payroll.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=cQZ0TmcY4hf9xT0k&q=85&s=5bba4eea1998a5ea84ac9357c81331fa)

* * *

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/common-use-cases/payroll#step-1-generate-your-api-keys)

Step 1: Generate your API Keys
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Head over to [**dashboard.bridge.xyz**](https://dashboard.bridge.xyz/)
. Once logged in, click on the “API Keys” tab on the top menu bar and generate a new API key. Bridge will make your **API key available only once**, so make sure to **immediately copy and save the key safely and securely**.  
  
Your key is used to authenticate into our APIs and is highly sensitive. If it ever gets compromised, you can immediately revoke key access from our dashboard and generate a new key.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/common-use-cases/payroll#step-2-onboard-a-customer)

Step 2: Onboard a customer
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a customer ID for each employer to manage payroll. Customers will need to accept our terms of service and complete KYC. Check out this [guide](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/introduction/quick-start/create-your-first-customer)
 for a full in depth explanation on onboarding customers. The below example walks you through using a KYC link to onboard your customer.

Request

    curl --location --request POST 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/kyc_links' \
    --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
    --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
    --header 'Idempotency-Key: <generate a uuid>' \
    --data-raw '{
      "full_name": "John Doe",
      "email": "johndoe@example.com",
      "type": "individual"
    }'
    

Response

    {
      "id": "uuid",
      "full_name": "John Doe",
      "email": "johndoe@example.com",
      "type": "individual", // or "business"
      "kyc_link": "https://bridge.withpersona.com/verify?",
      "tos_link": "https://dashboard.bridge.xyz/accept-terms-of-service?",
      "kyc_status": "not_started", // or "under_review", "incomplete", "approved" or "rejected"
      "rejection_reasons": [],
      "tos_status": "pending", // or "approved"
      "created_at": "2025-07-16T18:28:25.970Z",
      "customer_id": "customer_id",
      "persona_inquiry_type": "gov_id_db"
    }
    

Guide the user through:

1.  Visiting the `tos_link` and accepting terms of service
2.  Completing identity verification via the `kyc_link`

This process typically takes less than a minute and updates automatically once complete.

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/common-use-cases/payroll#step-3-create-a-wallet-for-the-employer)

Step 3: Create a wallet for the employer
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a wallet to hold the employer’s payroll funds.

Request

    curl --request POST \
         --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{employer-customer-id}/wallets \
         --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
         --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique Idempotency Key>' \
         --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
         --data '{
           "chain": "solana"
         }'
    

Response

    {
      "id": "employer-wallet-id-123",
      "chain": "solana",
      "address": "0x353253250000000001340033",
      "created_at": "2024-09-01T02:03:04.567Z",
      "updated_at": "2024-09-01T02:03:04.567Z"
    }
    

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/common-use-cases/payroll#step-4-create-a-wallet-for-an-employee)

Step 4: Create a wallet for an employee
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a wallet for each employee to get paid in stablecoins.

Request

    curl --request POST \
         --url https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/{employee-customer-id}/wallets \
         --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
         --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique Idempotency Key>' \
         --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
         --data '{
           "chain": "solana"
         }'
    

Response

    {
      "id": "employee-wallet-id-abc",
      "chain": "solana",
      "address": "0x444415153153500000120",
      "created_at": "2024-09-01T02:03:04.567Z",
      "updated_at": "2024-09-01T02:03:04.567Z"
    }
    

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/common-use-cases/payroll#step-5-create-a-virtual-account)

Step 5: Create a virtual account
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a USD or EUR account for the employer. Provide them with the bank instructions so they can deposit payroll. Deposits are converted to stablecoins and sent to their wallet. Use the [Virtual Accounts](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/virtual-accounts/create-a-virtual-account)
 API to provision permanent fiat deposit addresses for your customers. You define the `source` currency for the account and configure the `destination` to specify where Bridge should deliver the converted funds. Bridge handles the fiat-to-crypto conversion and sends the funds on-chain automatically.

Request

    curl --location --request POST 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/customers/<customer_id>/virtual_accounts' \
    --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
    --header 'Api-Key: <Api-Key>' \
    --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique Idempotency Key>' \
    --data-raw '{
      # The source object specifies a USD virtual account.
      "source": {
        "currency": "usd",
      },
      # You can specify the employer's wallet as the destination to receive funds
      "destination": {
        "payment_rail": "solana",
        "currency": "usdc",
        "bridge_wallet_id": "employer-wallet-id-123"
      }
    }'
    

[​](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/get-started/guides/common-use-cases/payroll#step-6-make-a-transfer)

Step 6: Make a transfer
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use the Transfers API to move funds from the employer’s wallet to the employee’s wallet. You will need to call the API for each employee. Use the [Transfers](https://apidocs.bridge.xyz/api-reference/transfers/create-a-transfer)
 API with the employer’s `bridge_wallet` as the source and the employee’s `bridge_wallet` as the destination.

Request

    curl --location --request POST 'https://api.bridge.xyz/v0/transfers' \
      --header 'Api-Key: <API Key>' \
      --header 'Idempotency-Key: <Unique Key>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data-raw '{
        "amount": "10.0",
        "on_behalf_of": "<customer_id>",
        "developer_fee": "0.0",
        "source": {
          "payment_rail": "bridge_wallet",
          "currency": "usdc",
          "bridge_wallet_id": "employer-wallet-id-123"
        },
        "destination": {
          "payment_rail": "solana",
          "currency": "usdc",
          "bridge_wallet_id": "employee-wallet-id-abc"
        }
      }'
    

Bridge will then initiate a crypto transfer from between the two specified bridge wallets.
